  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_941fc130-3fa6-4ccd-80a9-d1d64af409e6'

<span id="freeTextContainer3651669201163321884">Warning: This is not a story about fate or destiny. This is a story about pain, sorrow, and suffering. This is an impulsive whirlwind romance between two lovers that are not meant to be together. Theirs is not a world with sunshine and roses. Instead, their love blossoms in a secret world full of crime, violence, and death. Their story is about what can be born from nightm</span>
  <span id="freeText3651669201163321884" style="display:none">Warning: This is not a story about fate or destiny. This is a story about pain, sorrow, and suffering. This is an impulsive whirlwind romance between two lovers that are not meant to be together. Theirs is not a world with sunshine and roses. Instead, their love blossoms in a secret world full of crime, violence, and death. Their story is about what can be born from nightmares. <br /><br />Danielle “Danny” West is the daughter of Deuce West, President of the Hell’s Horsemen Motorcycle Club. A sweet and beautiful girl, she loses her way, searching for things that are always out of her reach. Erik “Ripper” Jacobs is the Sergeant of Arms in the Hell’s Horsemen. Once a man who always had a smile on his face, his life takes a turn for the worst when a tragedy befalls him, leaving him scarred and broken. During a midsummer night, Danny and Ripper’s paths cross, forever changing their lives. Hastily, their lust turns to love until another tragedy forces them apart. On a journey that is marred with ugliness and chaos, Danny and Ripper must discover if their unforeseen connection can find the beauty in their world. <br /><br />This is Danny and Ripper’s story. <br /><br />Everything has beauty. Even the ugly. Especially the ugly.<br />Because without ugly, there would be no beauty.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3651669201163321884" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<a href="/questions/464033-can-this-be-read-as-a-stand-alone-or-do-i">can this be read as a stand alone? or do i need to read the first book?</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_464033'><a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F16114861-unbeautifully">like</a></span>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/4169697-tinamarie"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1308313041i/4169697._UY100_CR14,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/4169697-tinamarie">TinaMarie</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
It can be read stand alone but it will have a lot more meaning if you read the first book as there is a lot of related story arcs in this book.
</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4826762570005727130"><b>Sweet Lord Jesus, new realms of awesomeness!!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769063.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is Danny and Ripper’s story:</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398121i/769064._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Please take a moment and let that sink in...<br/>...<br/>...<br/>...<br/><br/>Now close your eyes and imagine Deuce:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769065.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If you opened your eyes, say a little pray for Ripper's sorry ass or balls or any other part of his anatomy that he may need to function properly.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/562600.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>You’ll probably want to know some things before you start reading this (yeah, I'm pretty sure I'm talking to the one person who didn't get the chance to devour this book, yet): <br/>1. Go i</span>
  <span id="freeText4826762570005727130" style="display:none"><b>Sweet Lord Jesus, new realms of awesomeness!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769063.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is Danny and Ripper’s story:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398121i/769064._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Please take a moment and let that sink in...<br>...<br>...<br>...<br><br>Now close your eyes and imagine Deuce:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769065.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you opened your eyes, say a little pray for Ripper's sorry ass or balls or any other part of his anatomy that he may need to function properly.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/562600.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You’ll probably want to know some things before you start reading this (yeah, I'm pretty sure I'm talking to the one person who didn't get the chance to devour this book, yet): <br>1. Go inform your neighbors that they don't need to call the police or an ambulance if they hear you kicking and screaming, laughing like a hyena or crying like a lunatic.<br>2. Grab a swear jar, you're going to be rich.<br>3. Reel it in (I dare you to).<br>4. Do not go bat-shit crazy 'cause you need the next book "NOW!", we all do (I know, it sucks major balls)<br>5. Re-read point 3.<br>6. If you’re still feeling hormonal because you devoured Unbeautifully in less than 24 hours and now you have to wait some more for Unattainable, repeat after me: “I will have Shandor in a month!”<br>7. If you don’t know who Shandor is, well… grab me by the handle and call me Pan (it’s a Romanian saying for: “Are you shitting me?”)<br>8. Did I make you curious? GOOD!<br>9. Make sure you have an electrical tooth brush available.<br>10. Re-read point 3 or leave a message to Madeline <s>cursing</s> thanking her for ruining you for eternity and beyond. BTW: Did I tell you, Madeline, how much I <s>hate</s> love you!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>In three words I can sum up everything I’ve learned about life: it goes on. <br>—Robert Frost</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Let yourself sucked in to a hasty, impetuous, disastrous story that brings the ugly with the beauty, the scarred and broken with the sweet and delicate. As always, Madeline breaks the rules of a picture-perfect romance. <br><br><b>WARNING: <i>There are no rules when it comes to love.</i></b><br><br>Undeniable left us wanting <b>MORE</b>. Thank fuck we got it and we'll keep getting it. Undeniable didn't quite finish with "...and they lived happily ever after", because lets face it, shit happened and the name's Frankie. <br>We all know by now what Frankie did to Ripper. In Unbeautifully we get a glimpse of what really went down and how Ripper got away with a shattered exterior but still much alive, unfortunately that wasn't his plan. He wanted to die. Yeah, things don't work that way, and love doesn't happen like it really should.<br>Here is when Danny comes into the picture. She may seem preoccupied with appearances and <b>
  <i>always rambling on and on about music and clothes and some asshat named Chan-a-something Tater Tots.</i>
</b> , but her heart knows the difference from beauty and perfection.<br><br>These 2+tequila+skinny-dipping=TROUBLE<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398121i/769066.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And me???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769067.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Was it just me or was UnB <b>
  <i>hotter</i>
</b> than UnD??!! Maybe I was too shocked while reading UnD and didn't savor the hotness of it. But now in UnB I was like: <i>"Oh, you're in love with a man 14 years older than you. Bitch, try 18 years older. Oh, you think Mama Vi is scary, does Frankie ring your crazy bell?!"</i> So... yeah, I was more aware of how many times I was crackin' moisties. <br><br>Don't get me wrong, I was scared shitless of Ripper, that man was over 6 feet tall, bulged all over, missing an eye, scarred like he just survived a shark attack and had an attitude that you wouldn't want to fuck around with. But then he peed girly style and all was right in the world again. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>...he, a self-proclaimed drunken, gun-wielding, biker extraordinaire, plopped his ass down on the seat, tucked his dick between his legs, and pissed like a girl.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398121ra/769068.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book doesn't lack in fucked-upness, it's the same style we grew accustomed to and that we absolutely and undeniably LOVE!!! Not going to say more, because you have to be Frankie-crazy to not want to read this book.<br>I was so happy that we got a little more Deuce (lets face it, he's the big Kahuna and he can't be left out). But who's making himself noticed more and more in this book? Yep. It's the little Kahuna himself, Cage (my new favorite slut).<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Little fucker is almost as big as the big fucker.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Because there's no denying that Madeline Sheehan is the mother queen of all teasing, we get a little Cage here, then there and of course some more over there, too. Don't you dare expect me to reel it in and not go bananas after the next book, it's all your fault.<br><br>That being said, I just want to tell Madeline that she's the SHIT. I LOVE YOU!!! Please continue making hearts stop, bitches hate, jaws drop and panties wet. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398121i/769069._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/648282.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer3507690615030740197">*Warning: This book contains several aspects of the uglier side of life; it is not for everyone.*<br/><br/>Madeline's warning is true. Oh so true. But you know what? A pretty book does not necessarily make for a good book. A GREAT book even. Madeline's writing is honest, brutally honest. And unfuckingbelievable. <br/><br/>Somehow I kissed an angel's ass or something, because Madeline called me one night and was like "hey bitch... I need you to read this." Okay, if you know Madeline, first you don't say no. Second y</span>
  <span id="freeText3507690615030740197" style="display:none">*Warning: This book contains several aspects of the uglier side of life; it is not for everyone.*<br /><br />Madeline's warning is true. Oh so true. But you know what? A pretty book does not necessarily make for a good book. A GREAT book even. Madeline's writing is honest, brutally honest. And unfuckingbelievable. <br /><br />Somehow I kissed an angel's ass or something, because Madeline called me one night and was like "hey bitch... I need you to read this." Okay, if you know Madeline, first you don't say no. Second you are stupid to say no to this opportunity. Third, ARE YOU FUCKING KIDDING ME? Asked to dip into Unbeautifully early and give my honest opinion? Yep, I definitely got lucky. Really lucky. I owe someone a blow job for this.<br /><br />Anyway. Unbeautifully is the story of Danny and Ripper and the rest of Hell’s Horsemen Motorcycle Club guys and gals. Deuce and Eva are back too. Madeline came into her own in this book, outdoing herself with this plot and writing. Not for the faint of heart, but for the readers that will go balls to the walls in their reading.<br /><br />I stayed up all night reading this book... and literally texted Madeline in the middle of the night and I quote, "Ah me so horny. Love you long time." (Note to authors: don't give me your number if you don't want random texts while I'm reading.)<br /><br />This book was incredible. Amazing. Better than Undeniable (yeah, I said that). Danny and Ripper are hot. We get some more insight into Deuce and Eva. We get a taste of where we are going with Unattainable. I love these bad ass bikers and their old ladies. It's ugly. It's dirty. It's honest. It's sexy. It's steamy. It's beautifully Unbeautifully. </span>

<div id="review_494244604" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/494244604" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/494244604?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer494244604" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13108465010859121314"><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"We existed in a world where words weren't needed. Everything I needed to know, everything he was feeling, I could already see on his face and feel through his touch."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><p><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403358ra/784698.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Love is a feeling, a real, raw, and unscripted emotion so sensationally pure, unable to dull even under the strain of a world against it, strong enough to heal the broken and warm even the coldest of hearts.<br/><b>Innate.<br/>Unavoidable.<br/>Undeniable.</b></i><br/><br/>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br/><br/>Madeline Sheehan has written another </p></span>
  <span id="freeText13108465010859121314" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"We existed in a world where words weren't needed. Everything I needed to know, everything he was feeling, I could already see on his face and feel through his touch."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403358ra/784698.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Love is a feeling, a real, raw, and unscripted emotion so sensationally pure, unable to dull even under the strain of a world against it, strong enough to heal the broken and warm even the coldest of hearts.<br><b>Innate.<br>Unavoidable.<br>Undeniable.</b></i><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br>Madeline Sheehan has written another <b>FAN-fucking-TASTIC, EMOTIONAL, GUT WRENCHING, SOUL SHATTERING, HEARTWARMING, UNPUTDOWNABLE</b> story that I absolutely LOVED reading. <br><br>Just like <i>Undeniable</i>, <b>Unbeautifully</b> is a real, raw, gritty and intense story. From the moment I started reading it, it sucked me in and kept me up until the wee hours of the morning because I simply could not stop reading it!! It wasn't always an easy story to read; some parts of it were downright hurtful and messy, but in the end the beauty of it far outweighed the ugly and to me, that's all that truly matters. <i>Unbeautifully</i> is the kind of story that will <b>unavoidably, undeniably</b> keep you glued to the pages until you've reached the final page and everything finally clicks into place in the most beautiful way possible.<br><br><br><b>Unbeautifully</b> is the story of Danny and Ripper...<br><br><i>Ours was the furthest thing from a picture-perfect romance; it was more of a car crash, a metal-bending, blood-spattered disaster that left no survivors, only bad memories and heartache.<br>But it was ours.<br>And because it was ours...I wouldn't chance a thing.</i><br><br>The story picks up right where the events of Undeniable ended. Danielle "Danny" West, Deuce's oldest daughter is now twenty one years old and she's the girlfriend of one of her dad's club's members, ZZ. At a summer barbeque ZZ proposes to her but right before she's about to answer him, the story shifts back to three years earlier. After that, we follow the events that led up to that moment, a moment in which Danny will have to chose between ZZ and Ripper...<br><br><b><u>Danny --</u></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403358i/784699._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As an eighteen year old girl, Danny feels lonely and miserable after everything that happened with her family. Her mother left her at an early age and her father Deuce, although he loves her and would do anything to protect his children, isn't exactly a role model kind of dad which pretty much left her and her brother Cage to grow up by themselves. Al these events have made her into a strong, mature young woman, but at the same time she's also struggling to find out what to do with her life. On her prom night, Ripper was sent to pick her up from the dance, but on their way home, they make a stop at a lake, because Danny doesn't want to go home yet and one thing leads to another... <br><br><b><i>"Danny," he growled, refusing to look at her. "You keep touchin' me like that and I ain't gonna be responsible for what I end up doin'."<br><br>And then he heard it. Five little words that shut off his brain and spurred his body into action. "Ripper," she whispered against his ruined skin. "Make my prom night perfect."</i></b><br><br>She wanted him to make her prom night special and just for once, forget about all the misery in her life, and that's exactly what he did. They spend one blissful night together and assumed they'll be able to pretend nothing happened the next day. But something changed that night for the both of them, it was a night neither of them is able to get out of their head and as the weeks grow, they realize they've developed feeling for each other. <br><br><b><i>"Whatever he wanted me to do, whatever he wanted to do to me, I already knew the answer would be a thousand times yes. I was at a point of no return."</i></b><br><br><b><u>Ripper --</u></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403358i/784700._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ripper is a man with a broken past. After batshit crazy Frankie got his hands on him, he's ruined on the outside. He has so many scars on the outside, and it feels like his ruined on the outside too. Other than the Club, his life doesn't seem to have much meaning. Until he meets the beautiful, young, vibrant Danielle...<br><br><b><i>"All scars tell a story, beautiful girl," he said. "And mine," he said softly, grabbing my hand, trailing my palm across his cheek and then his chest. "Tell the story of how I found you."</i></b><br><br>Ripper's always had his fair share of women, but he's never truly cared about a woman before, never been in love, until Danny...<br><br><b><i>"But Danny was different.<br>A game changer."</i></b><br><br>Danny finally makes him see that although he's all scarred up on the outside; those scars don't make him any less beautiful. Shee makes him feel alive and determined to truly start living again after feeling miserable and rather wishing he were dead for a very long time. He realizes he loved Danny, but their love is unconventional. They're not "supposed to" be together. Ripper is fourteen years older than Danny and a member of her father's motorcycle club and both of them *know* Deuce will never allow them to be together... They have to sneak around and when things start to get out of hand, their affair become messy and highly emotional.<br><br>But is that enough to keep them apart, or will their love prevail and make them strong enough to fight the odds and fight for what they both deserve?<br><br><b><i>"It didn't make any sense. Did love make sense? Oh god, it was all too much. But like most things involving Ripper and me, they were always impulsive, messy, and confusing, giving new meaning to the term <u>whirlwind romance<u>."</u></u></i></b><br><br>Aside from Danny and Ripper's story we also get a background story with scenes from Eva and Deuce's POV. After what happened with Frankie, the guy who singlehandedly ruined a dozen people's lives, both of them are still struggling to go back to the way things were <i>before Frankie</i>. I loved the fact that Eva and Deuce still had a big part in this story and that they eventually get the HEA they both deserve so much. At the same time we also get a lot of background stories on the other bikers and their crazy-ass lives like the one of Cox and Kami (still going at each other like crazy), Jase and Dorothy (who have a tragic history of their own) and Cage (who's kind of a man whore but also a hottie and whose story I'm already anxiously awaiting!) ;-)<br><br>Madeline Sheehan writes epic, badass biker stories like nobody else and I can't wait to read the rest of this magnificent series!<br><br></p><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403358ra/784701.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But of course the main focus in <i>Unbeautifully</i> is still on Ripper and Danny and their tragically beautiful and heartfelt story full of pain, misery and suffering but in the end it all comes down to one thing: LOVE.<br></p><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Ripper," I whispered, clinging to his neck as he carried me from the bathroom into his bedroom. " I think I love you."<br><br>"Yeah, baby," he whispered, sliding back inside of me. "Ain't no other explanation for what a girl like you is doin' in bed with a man like me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403358i/784702.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Baby," he said gruggly. "Man like me got no business with a girl like you. You're nothin' but fuckin' beauty and I'm a whole lot of fuckin' ugly who's already halfway to hell."<br><br>But he was wrong.<br>Everything has beauty. Even the ugly. Especially the ugly.<br>Because without the ugly, there would be no beauty.<br>Because without beauty, we would not survive our pain, our sorrow, and our suffering.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403358ra/784703.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
</p><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You may not be beautiful the way you were before," I whispered, cupping his ruined cheek. "But you're still beautiful. To me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>If you haven't read this series yet, <u>READ IT</u> and fall in love with these beautifully flawed characters Madeline Sheehan has created and that will stay with me for a very long time. <b>Unbeautifully</b> is a more than worthy sequel to the epic story of Undeniable and personally, I loved it even more than Eva and Deuce's story. ♥<br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403358ra/784704.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>5 BEAUTIFULLY CAPTIVATING STARS.</b>
  <br>
</p></span>
  <a data-text-id="13108465010859121314" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer449934592" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6142704770692956906"><b>3.5 stars.****Review completed May 16, 2013</b><br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396733i/765035.png' alt=' photo Bildschirmfoto2013-05-13um191106_zps19d2ef9b.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>…we came together in a frantic rush of skin and limbs, my magnitude of need an all-consuming burn that I needed…needed…god, I just needed all of him, touching all of me.<br/> <br/>"Baby," he said. "Listen to me. I ain't beautiful, you are. You're so damn beautiful you got it spillin' out all over the place, blinding' you into thinkin' I'm beautiful when I ain't. Farthest thing from it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396733ra/765036.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mji9x2jyio1s33inqo1_500_zpse4476e16.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Meant what I said," he said, dropping his head, press</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText6142704770692956906" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars.****Review completed May 16, 2013</b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396733i/765035.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-05-13um191106_zps19d2ef9b.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>…we came together in a frantic rush of skin and limbs, my magnitude of need an all-consuming burn that I needed…needed…god, I just needed all of him, touching all of me.<br> <br>"Baby," he said. "Listen to me. I ain't beautiful, you are. You're so damn beautiful you got it spillin' out all over the place, blinding' you into thinkin' I'm beautiful when I ain't. Farthest thing from it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396733ra/765036.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mji9x2jyio1s33inqo1_500_zpse4476e16.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Meant what I said," he said, dropping his head, pressing his forehead to mine. "You're with me, you're with only me. I ain't gonna share you with some teenage asshat whose dick ain't full grown."<br> <br>"No, baby, I'm not. I'm tryin' to figure out whether I'm gonna slap some sense into you or fuck the shit outta you."<br> <br>…we came together in a frantic rush of skin and limbs, my magnitude of need an all-consuming burn that I needed…needed…god, I just needed all of him, touching all of me.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396733ra/765037.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mkgeihMjEy1r1etb2o1_500_zpsee99725b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Ripper," I whispered, clinging to his neck as he carried me from the bathroom into his bedroom. "I think I love you."<br>Laying me gently down on his bed, he climbed over top of me and covered me with his body.<br>"Yeah, baby," he whispered, sliding back inside of me. "Ain't no other explanation for what a girl like you is doin' in bed with a man like me."<br> <br>"Yeah, beautiful girl," he whispered. "I'm feelin' you too."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396734ra/765038.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mevvk5gj4Z1qdunk8o1_500_zps3f41b561.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"FUCK YOU!" He roared as his fist shot out. The mirror shattered on impact.<br>Shattered.<br>Just like his fucking life.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396734ra/765039.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mjj1n4HwqQ1rbgv4do1_500_zps35679c48.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Jesus. Why couldn't he have had boys? All boys. Little fucking shits like Cage. A whole slew of 'em he could throw condoms at and be done with it.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396734ra/765040.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mdmkukSSHQ1r8ufr0o1_500_zps9b42e61b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Rainstorms brought you to your knees, soaking you in uncontrollable need, lightning flashing before your eyes while you dug your fingers deep into the earth, trying to hold on; unable to tell which was louder…the thunder roaring in your ears or the pounding of your heart.<br>Ripper was my rainstorm, my skin-drenching frenzy, where you couldn't tell right from left, where all you could feel was the phenomenon exploding throughout your body, feverishly burning through you even as it pleasurably cooled.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396734ra/765041.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_md2xnp5m4n1qj73e2o1_500_zps49196aac.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>The most difficult reviews to write are those where you neither loved nor hated a book. I’m sitting in front of my laptop, perusing my mind to find the right words and I feel underwhelmed and uninspired. Well, here we go. I’m trying to make it short and to the point though.<br> <br>First off, the ‘quotes’ I added to my review are the most “interesting” I could find in Unbeautifully, and since I’m a sucker for great quotes it says a lot that my eye couldn’t catch more. In fact, it’s a little bit disappointing. What will always stay with me, however, are the never ending and excessive temper tantrums. In a nutshell Unbeautifully provided plenty of sobbing and crying, OTT hysterical and screeching women that hurt my ears and caused me a headache, plenty of male and female shouting as well as <i>drama over drama over drama.</i> Hence, I was ready to fall on my knees and beg: Just. Tone. It. Down. A. Little. Bit. Also, the sex in this book didn’t do anything for me. Mostly it was about f@ck--me--through--the--mattress or f@ck--me--through--the--wall encounters. Or whatever. Honestly, it didn’t knock me on <b>my</b> ass. I mean that might be good and enjoyable a couple times but then it gets old and boring pretty quickly. Readers who loved Deuce in Undeniable will get an eyeful, earful and mouthful of him and his <i>
  <b>oh-so smart</b>
</i> Eva in Unbeautifully. Witnessing their antics was strenuous and yet totally diverting, I’ll give them that. However, I can’t for the life of me understand why Eva has been described as smart coz she was anything but. Truth be told I couldn’t believe my eyes when I read <i>that:</i><br> <br><i>“There is an old story passed down through the generations of a Native American grandfather counseling his young grandson, telling him that he has two wolves living inside of him, constantly fighting each other for dominance. One is the wolf of peace, love and kindness. The other represents fear, greed, and hatred. The boy asks, ‘Which wolf will win, Grandfather?’ and the wise old man replies ‘Whichever one I feed.”<br>Eva stared at her, wondering what the woman was talking about.</i><br> <br>Um…clue the f@ck in, Eva, you dumb twit! Yup, you are such a <i>smart</i> ‘bitch’. *major headdesk moment* There’s no getting round it to point out that I slightly resent it when female characters come across as dumb, whiny, needy, and overly hysterical (this includes Danny too). It happened in Undeniable  and it was an ongoing issue in Unbeautifully as well.<br> <br>Unbeautifully should have been Ripper and Danny’s story, however, I got the impression that Deuce and Eva overshadowed the other couple all the time—certainly Deuce. And let’s face it, without Deuce Unbeautifully wouldn’t have been the same because he somehow made this story. Though I felt that the fallout of Eva’s <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[rape <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was not really dealt with. Deuce storming off all the time and attempting to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[have sex with another ‘bitch’ <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was weird, to say the least. After all, this is a major issue and dealing with it in a superficial way is neither believable nor ‘satisfying’. I would have expected to see them having a real conversation once in a while. Just sit down and work it out already! Geez, they were constantly avoiding the elephant in the room. That’s why I think it was a missed opportunity and everything was so nicely and quickly wrapped up in the end—delivered with a lovely bow actually. <i>’I want you back. I miss you.’</i> That’s so incredibly convenient and not good enough for me.<br> <br>I didn’t like the plot twist at 58 % when Ripper <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[simply left everything and everyone behind after Nikki had been killed. He didn’t say a word and his acting out led to their long separation and to Danny’s abortion AND to her hooking up with ZZ. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Stilted drama, much?<br> <br><b>What I liked</b><br>What I really appreciated about this book was the <i>
  <b>concept</b>
</i> of loving someone who is physically scarred and ugly, but when you look beyond the scars you can find beauty. After all, beauty is in the eye of the beholder and it comes in many different forms and shapes. Besides, beauty is arbitrary. It is not only about physical perfection, it’s an inner feeling and being loved will make you feel good and happy and in spite of all the scars it helps you to radiate beauty.<br> <br>Compared to Undeniable the editing of Unbeautifully was a major improvement which pleased me a lot.<br> <br>In conclusion, I liked and enjoyed Unbeautifully and its entertainment value is rather high, for sure, and yet I can't help but feel a tiny bit disappointed. It wasn’t a knockout.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396734ra/765042.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mgq9afA1pm1qigj88o1_500_zps5c78c612.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396734i/765043.jpg" alt=" photo 559b5cd0-5f2e-4c15-95dd-b5a07dc39687_zps28d0a255.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"All scars tell a story, beautiful girl," he said, releasing me to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[trace the marks on my stomach. "Yours are tellin' me how healthy and fuckin' perfect my kid is gonna be." <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>A tear slid out of the corner of my eye. "Shut up," I whispered.<br>"And mine," he said softly, grabbing my hand, trailing my palm across his cheek and then his chest. "Tell the story of how I found you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br> <br><b>Warning</b><br>If you are sensitive to explicit and graphic violence, torture and bloodshed, sex and swearing then this is <b>not</b> the book for you. The f-bomb is dropped in many different variations all the time and it’s very obvious that cussing is as vital as breathing in the badass biker world.<br> <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="6142704770692956906" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</a><br><br>OK So I know what your thinking… <i>(must read in whiny voice) “But KELLLLIIIIIIEEE You haven’t actually told us what happens in this book?” </i> <br>Well guess what suckers I’m not going to! <br>This book <b>HAS</b> to be read <br>So much happens that if I start to explain what happens, it won’t be a surprise! <br><br>I <b>WILL</b> tell you that <br><br>- &gt; <b>NO-ONE</b> writes like Madeline! <br><br>- &gt; We get <b>MORE</b> of Deuce and Eva. <br>- &gt; <b>NOTHING</b> is easy for Ripper and Danny! <br>- &gt; I <b>THINK</b> I like Ripper more than Deuce. <i>(It’s really hard to compare them both! And then there is Cage, and Hawk, and ZZ and jusy sigh)</i><br>- &gt;<b>Sex Scenes</b> are detailed, brutal and FAN-FUCKIN-TASTIC!<br>- &gt; We also get a <b>TEASE</b> about Tegan and Cage. <br>- &gt; Kami and Cox are still <b>CRAZY</b> Mo’Fo’s. <br>- &gt; There is a <b>TRIANGLE</b> of Hawk- Dorothy- Jase. <br>- &gt; <b>SOMETHING</b> horrible happens, but it is not a rape like in the first one<br>- &gt; It is takes place over <b>YEARS</b> but not as many as the first book. <br>- &gt; Ivy is so darn <b>CUTE</b> <br>- &gt; The sneak peek that we have all read about Eva and Deuce’s <b>WEDDING</b> is in there. <br>- &gt; It’s told in Eva, Deuce’s, Danny and Rippers <b>POV</b> <br>- &gt; And old <b>Blue</b> is still around. <br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/user/lil_kel4/media/beautiful%20lie%20reactions/myboyblue_zpsa31cd9cf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

Me.” <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#<br>“All scars tell a story, beautiful girl,” he said. “And mine,” he said softly, grabbing my hand,, trailing my palm across his cheek and then his chest. “Tell the story of how I found you.” <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#<br>“Ripper,” I whispered, clinging to his neck as he carried me from the bathroom into his bedroom. “I think I love you.” <br>“Yeah, baby,” he whispered, sliding back inside me. “Ain’t no other explanation for what a girl like you is doin’ in bed with a man like me.” <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#<br>“I wanna rip you the fuck open,” he said breathing harder as his thrusts became brutal. <br>“I want all of me inside you, not just my fucking cock baby, but all of me.” <br>“Yes,” she whimpered. “I want all of you.” <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#<br>“Meant what I said,” he said dropping his forehead to mine. “You’re with me, your only with me. I ain’t gonna share you with some teenage asshat whose dick ain’t full grown.” <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#<br>“Yeah beautiful girl,” he whispered. “I’m feeling you too.” <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#<br>Jesus. Why couldn’t he have had boys? All boys? Little fucking shits like Cage. A whole slew of ‘em he could throw condoms at and be done with it. <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#<br>“If your old man caps me, you better be front and center at my fuckin’ funeral, crying your goddamn eyes out.” <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#<br>“Motherfuck,” Deuce muttered, staring after him. “Ten bucks says he fucked that mouthy little asshole. She was always rambling on and on about music and clothes and some asshat named Chan-a-something Tater Tots.” <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#<br>“Babe,” he whispered. “Can’t look at me like that and expect me to be keepin’ it reeled in.”<br>“Baby, don’t ever keep it reeled in,” she whispered back. “Not with me.” <br>#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*#*# </b><br><br>OK so I highlighted a lot more than that but I'll leave it at that before I write the whole book on here. <br>Just *sigh* READ THIS FUCKING BOOK! <br><br>BRING ON THE NEXT!!!<br><br>***oct 30/12**<b>2 MORE BOOKS TO COME?!?! <br>HELLS YEAH!!!</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1150.photobucket.com/albums/o606/lil_kel4/?action=view&amp;current=airhump.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_443929059" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/443929059" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/443929059?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=actiony">actiony</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own-signed">pb-i-own-signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=dark-n-gritty">dark-n-gritty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=bikers">bikers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer443929059" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17901579888011449742"><b>Another sensational read from Madeline Sheehan. <br/>AND GODDAMN, I WANT A HOT, BADASS, FOUL-MOUTHED BIKER BOY!!!</b><br/><br/>Danny and Ripper…<br/><br/><i>“Ours was the furthest thing from a picture-perfect romance; it was more of a car crash, a metal-bending, blood-splattered disaster that left no survivors, only bad memories and heartache. <br/>But it was ours.<br/>And because it was ours…I wouldn’t change a thing.”</i><br/><br/>That quote came from the prologue of this book. By the end of the prologue, I was hooked. By the end of the first chapt</span>
  <span id="freeText17901579888011449742" style="display:none"><b>Another sensational read from Madeline Sheehan. <br />AND GODDAMN, I WANT A HOT, BADASS, FOUL-MOUTHED BIKER BOY!!!</b><br /><br />Danny and Ripper…<br /><br /><i>“Ours was the furthest thing from a picture-perfect romance; it was more of a car crash, a metal-bending, blood-splattered disaster that left no survivors, only bad memories and heartache. <br />But it was ours.<br />And because it was ours…I wouldn’t change a thing.”</i><br /><br />That quote came from the prologue of this book. By the end of the prologue, I was hooked. By the end of the first chapter, I had already rated 5 stars and was bouncing up and down in my chair, so freaking excited to read the rest of the book.<br /><br />Fair warning too - I’ve gone all quote-whore in my review again. Deal with it :P<br /><br />This book starts where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16109563.Undeniable__Undeniable___1_" title="Undeniable (Undeniable, #1) by Madeline Sheehan" rel="nofollow noopener">Undeniable</a> finishes, and we are straight back into the world of the Hell’s Horsemen MC. Deuce and Eva are (at last) happily married, and Deuce’s daughter Danny, and club member, Ripper have some INTENSE chemistry going on, but despite all of the eye fuckery, there is some major animosity between them. They clearly have history, and there is one EPIC moment, before the story moves back to three years previously to get the start of their story.<br /><br />As the daughter of a MC Prez, 18 year old Danny has grown up in the biker world. <i>“A world of constant crime and cruelty, a cold world full of despair and death.”</i>. She has always been a spirited, happy and vibrant girl, but with the fallout of the events at the end of <i>Undeniable</i> (before the HEA epilogue), her life has fallen to pieces, and she is struggling to cope. And then along comes Ripper. He has been left horrifically scarred after being brutally tortured in the first book, and is still nursing a whole heap of issues. At 32 years old, he is 14 years older than Danny, but the two of them come together unexpectedly one night, and it irrevocably alters them both. <br /><br />Unable to stay away from each other, they engage in a clandestine affair – kept secret because of Deuce’s club rules that nobody is to touch his baby girl. And above all else, Ripper is loyal to his club, his brothers, and to his President. <br /><br /><i>“He was fucked. He was so fucking fucked.” <br /><br />“If your old man caps me, you better be front and center at my fuckin’ funeral, cryin’ your goddamn eyes out.”</i><br /><br />Theirs is an intense and all consuming love. They fall fast, and they fall hard, and together they are absolutely SMOKING HOT!!! There is some sensational character development as the two of them find strength in each other, but one tragic event brings it all to a screeching halt. And in order to protect Danny, and thinking that she is better off without him (ugh, why do guys do that???), he takes off, shattering them both. <br /><br />Told in dual POV, we get to see both of them try to move on, and my heart broke over and over again at everything they went through, and the circumstances they are forced to deal with. And when they inevitably come face to face again, there is still so much feeling between them, their love and anger practically explode off the page, but there are even more obstacles between them now, and they still have so much more to face! There is lots of heartache, and plenty of ‘oh fuck’ moments, not only for Danny and Ripper, but for the rest of the MC, and it’s one helluva ride!<br /><br />“FUCK THIS SHIT.<br /><i>Fuck the club and the code, and fuck brotherhood. He would give it all up for her. For his woman. Because she sure as shit was his, and he’d go to hell and back ten times over before he lost her forever.</i>”<br /><br />And oh joy, there is a lots of Deuce and Eva time! The majority of this book is retrospective, and so we get to see them suffering through the after effects of the ending of <i>Undeniable</i>. And it is utterly heartbreaking! Seeing them so torn up after everything that they had been through was just devastating! But thank God, we got to see the moment where it all turns around for them, and even though I knew the outcome, I was still cheering. <br /><br /><i>“I love you,” she cried softly. “No one else, baby, not like this, not the way I’ve always loved you.”<br />“How much do you love me?” he asked hoarsely …<br />“You already know,” she whimpered. “You’re everything to me, everything, you always have been, baby…” <br /><br />“Eva,” he rasped, cupping the back of her head and forcing her to look at him. “Marry me, darlin’.” </i><br /><br />And a big shout out to Danny’s big brother Cage. He’s a total manwhore…<br /><br /><i>“Motherfuck,” Deuce muttered, staring after him. “Ten bucks says he fucked that mouthy little asshole. Motherfuckin’ little fuck can’t keep it in his pants for shit. Cocksucker would fuck a hole in the wall. Probably has.”</i><br /><br />… but he is beautifully protective of his baby sister. <br /><br /><i>“Coulda fuckin’ told me, little sister,” he said quietly. “Would never let you go through all this shit by yourself.”<br />Grabbing my hand, he threaded his large fingers through mine and squeezed. “This is what big brothers are fuckin’ here for … To pick their little sisters up when they fall the fuck down.”</i><br /><br />He's a total mini-Deuce and I love him. His story is set up very nicely, and I'm excited for the fireworks which I am sure are to come!<br /><br />There are other storylines woven throughout the book involving the other members of the MC. It’s good, it’s bad, and it’s shocking, but it all adds to the biker world, and to the reality of the lifestyle. And the banter between the boys is sensational!<br /><br /><i>“Who’s fuckin’ pussy-whipped now, asshat?” Cox laughed over his shoulder. “That would be you, bitch!”<br />“You did not just call me a bitch!” Mick roared, chasing him. <br />“Bitch! I fuckin’ did! Bitch!”</i><br /><br />While, for me, this book didn’t have the shocking ‘in-your-face-what-the-fuck-did-I-just-read?’ punch that <i>Undeniable</i> did, it is still an absolutely fantastic book. The writing is phenomenal, it’s vivid and real, and completely sucks you into the story. And once again, Madeline pulls no punches when creating her biker world. It’s dirty, brutal, violent, and shocking at times, yet the bond of the brotherhood is incredibly strong, and she still manages to make you care about her characters – even when they do horribly deplorable things. Plus we get not one, but two beautiful (although slightly fucked up) love stories featuring four broken, but incredible characters that are absolutely unforgettable. <br /><br />I loved every single moment of this book, I wish it was longer. 5 sensational stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17901579888011449742" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_443758052" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/443758052" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/443758052?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer443758052" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12211499097550153602"><b>5 Phenomenal Stars! </b><br/><br/>When I read Undeniable last year, I was blown away. It was raw, gritty, intense... and I loved every second! This book was no different. I was hooked from the prologue. One of those books you will not be able to put down.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/dccd1cc4-0484-45a6-9560-c91519b6a912_zpsf658d2ff.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395789i/762408.jpg' alt=' photo dccd1cc4-0484-45a6-9560-c91519b6a912_zpsf658d2ff.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is Danny and Ripper’s story. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/7ec39963-fa75-4557-b5b6-527249a60b53_zpsc2df7c83.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395789i/762409.jpg' alt=' photo 7ec39963-fa75-4557-b5b6-527249a60b53_zpsc2df7c83.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Danielle West grew up with Deuce as a father. Deuce is the Prez of the local MC club. Things haven’t been ideal at home. Her mom has been out of the picture for some time, her dad and step-mom have been having their i</span>
  <span id="freeText12211499097550153602" style="display:none"><b>5 Phenomenal Stars! </b><br><br>When I read Undeniable last year, I was blown away. It was raw, gritty, intense... and I loved every second! This book was no different. I was hooked from the prologue. One of those books you will not be able to put down.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/dccd1cc4-0484-45a6-9560-c91519b6a912_zpsf658d2ff.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395789i/762408.jpg" alt=" photo dccd1cc4-0484-45a6-9560-c91519b6a912_zpsf658d2ff.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is Danny and Ripper’s story. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/7ec39963-fa75-4557-b5b6-527249a60b53_zpsc2df7c83.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395789i/762409.jpg" alt=" photo 7ec39963-fa75-4557-b5b6-527249a60b53_zpsc2df7c83.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Danielle West grew up with Deuce as a father. Deuce is the Prez of the local MC club. Things haven’t been ideal at home. Her mom has been out of the picture for some time, her dad and step-mom have been having their issues. Her brother is out manwhoring. She has had to step up at home a lot to help with her little sister Ivy. Her family is falling apart. It’s her senior year of high school and she is eighteen. At her high school prom. She calls the club for a ride home, she is ready to get out of there. Ripper comes to pick her up. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/20f987e0-571b-41aa-90d1-579fe431f043_zpse8db3f2d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395789i/762410._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 20f987e0-571b-41aa-90d1-579fe431f043_zpse8db3f2d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ripper has been through hell. Not only did he lose his family at a young age, the last 5 years have been especially difficult. After being cut up and scarred by crazy Frankie, he harbors a lot of resentment. When he picks Danny up, he insists she dances. Its her prom. She wants to dance with him. Once they leave, she’s not ready to go home. Against his better judgement, he takes her to the lake. He knows they shouldn’t, but things happen between the two of them.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Baby, man like me got no business with a girl like you. You’re nothin’ but fuckin’ beauty and I’m a whole lot of fuckin’ ugly who’s halfway to hell.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Ripper knows he isn’t good enough for Danny, but he can’t stop wanting her. He keeps his distance... she is Prez’s daughter and he knows to pursue her would be suicide. She wears down all his defenses. She sees past the scars, sees him.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Ripper, you’re still beautiful. So you’ve got some scars. So what?”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Weeks go by, and they keep their distance. Finally, they can’t stay away any longer. With Deuce and some of the others away on business, Danny and Ripper spend a magical week together holed up in his cabin. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/2c6a3032-6fe3-4165-863c-e23f8609f01f_zps8e23924f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395789i/762411.jpg" alt=" photo 2c6a3032-6fe3-4165-863c-e23f8609f01f_zps8e23924f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Danny starts to fall for Ripper. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Ripper, I think I love you.”<br> “Yeah, baby. Ain’t no other explanation for what a girl like you is doin’ in bed with a man like me.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Danny wants to tell her father about their relationship, she wants to tell everyone. Ripper knows how dangerous that would be. He insists they stay quiet. But he can’t fight his feelings. He is falling for Danny too. He finally found someone that might be worth changing his ways for. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Erik Jacobs had finally fallen for a woman. </blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/b9655f9d-e624-472f-bc32-5d21016851ea_zps9add0172.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395789i/762412.jpg" alt=" photo b9655f9d-e624-472f-bc32-5d21016851ea_zps9add0172.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>But loyalty means everything to Ripper. He is a brother. Things get a little sketchy from here...<br><br>I am going to stop summarizing there... you really have to read this one. I will tell you this. Shit gets crazy! <br><br>We get a lot of Eva and Deuce, some Cox and Kami, Cage, and a ton of other characters from the first book. It was really great to catch up will all of them and see their stories. You know I love me some Deuce...<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I’m gonna fix it, and then I’m gonna fix it again and keep on fixin it until the bad stops outweighin’ the good, until there ain’t nothin’ but good left.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>This book/series is a must read. It has angst, action, love, sex, grit, and intensity. This was amazing and is for sure going right on my favorites shelf. I think I loved Danny &amp; Ripper’s story even more than Deuce &amp; Eva’s. I loved those two. My feelings were all over the place while reading, but I loved every single second of this book! I will say it again... these books are MUST READS! If you haven’t read them... do it now! You are seriously missing out! <br><br>Madeline Sheehan you are most awesome for creating this world with these crazy, intense, yet lovable characters! The writing was fantastic as always. I can’t flippin’ wait for the next book... CAGE- yes please!!! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I am leary about it being Cage and Tegen’s book... I really couldn’t stand her in this one. But I’m sure Madeline will make me love her!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/b89e054a-1687-4623-8ced-6bb0dcee4687_zps6140266c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395789i/762413.jpg" alt=" photo b89e054a-1687-4623-8ced-6bb0dcee4687_zps6140266c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>“All scars tell a story, beautiful girl. And mine, tell the story of how I found you.”</blockquote>
</b><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer446095295" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13437599666892095012"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396141i/763368._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>How does Madeline Sheehan write this series? <br/> <br/>My only guess is that she must be the ‘prez’ of her local biker club and if so…patch me in babe!<br/><br/>Ms. Sheehan writes foulmouthed hardcore bikers like nobody’s business!!<br/> <br/>I'm still reeling myself in…from this gritty, raw, funny, flawed, dirty and intense ride with the Horsemen! <i>Unbeautifully</i> was absolutely FAN-FREAKIN-TASTIC!!!<br/><br/>The story takes place immediately following the ending of <i>Undeniable</i>. We back track to see how beautiful Danielle West, daughter</span>
  <span id="freeText13437599666892095012" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396141i/763368._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How does Madeline Sheehan write this series? <br> <br>My only guess is that she must be the ‘prez’ of her local biker club and if so…patch me in babe!<br><br>Ms. Sheehan writes foulmouthed hardcore bikers like nobody’s business!!<br> <br>I'm still reeling myself in…from this gritty, raw, funny, flawed, dirty and intense ride with the Horsemen! <i>Unbeautifully</i> was absolutely FAN-FREAKIN-TASTIC!!!<br><br>The story takes place immediately following the ending of <i>Undeniable</i>. We back track to see how beautiful Danielle West, daughter of Deuce, club president falls for Ripper and finds herself in the position of being proposed to by ZZ at a barbeque.<br><br>The prologue kicked major ass and a fan will be sucked right back into this world that Ms. Sheehan has masterfully created.<br><br>We see and feel all the ramifications of Frankie’s terror spree on our characters and all of the scars that the victims bare. I felt their struggle and I celebrated as they slowly took their lives back.<br><br>We get so much of Deuce and Eva and then theres crazy Kami and Cox (hysterical couple) Old Blue (your still my boy), Dirty (loved him), Cage is smokin’ hot can’t wait for his book, and of course we fall in love with Ripper and Dani.<br><br>Ripper and Dani had CHEMISTRY and so much more! Ripper was a victim of Frankie. He bares horrific scars and has been broken and depressed ever since. On Dani’s prom night he gives her a ride home, and well the rest is history…<br> <br><b>
  <i>“Baby, man like me got no business with a girl like you. You’re nothin’ but fuckin’ beauty and I’m a whole lot of fuckin’ ugly who’s halfway to hell.” ~ Ripper</i>
</b><br><br>The couple sneak around due to Ripper’s fear of Deuce finding out and killing him. They find the forever kind of love and it’s Sexy and Beautiful! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396141i/763369._SY540_.jpg" width="360" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>”Ripper”, I whispered, clinging to his neck as he carried me from the bathroom into his bedroom. “I think I love you.” ~ Dani<br><br><b><i>”Yeah baby”, he whispered, sliding back inside me. “Aint no other explanation for what a girl like you is doin’ in bed with a man like me.”~ Ripper</i></b></i>
  <br>
  <br>
</b>A whole lot of terrible things happen to Dani and Ripper along with some horrible decisions. I was frustrated, angry and crushed by their actions. <br> <br><b>
  <i>"It was all there, everything he was feeling everything I needed to know, written all over his face.<br>He loved me.<br>And he hated me."</i>
</b><br><br>This love story is anything but perfect. But it was real, raw, heartbreaking and beautiful. I routed for them and I cried at their pain and I struggled alongside them to get our hea.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Love is a feeling, a real, raw, and unscripted emotion so sensationally pure, unable to dull even under the strain of a world against it, strong enough to heal the broken and warm even the coldest hearts.<br>Innate.<br>Unavoidable.<br>Undeniable.”</i>
</b><br><br>I love you hard Madeline Sheenan! </span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/444849383?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer444849383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12906822705842289124"><b>4+ Scarred but still Shining, Beauty and Love Stars<br/><br/><i>Everything has beauty. Even the ugly. Especially the ugly. Because without ugly, there would be no beauty. Because without beauty, we would not survive our pain, our sorrow, and our suffering.</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762923.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762924.png' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Once upon a time a girl, <b>Danielle "Danny" West</b> fell in love with a tortured man, <b>Erik “Ripper” Jacobs</b> who loved her more than his scarred heart dared to admit.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762925.png' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Danny, the daughter of the President of Hell’s Horsemen Motorcycle Club was supposed to get away o</span>
  <span id="freeText12906822705842289124" style="display:none"><b>4+ Scarred but still Shining, Beauty and Love Stars<br><br><i>Everything has beauty. Even the ugly. Especially the ugly. Because without ugly, there would be no beauty. Because without beauty, we would not survive our pain, our sorrow, and our suffering.</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762923.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762924.png" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Once upon a time a girl, <b>Danielle "Danny" West</b> fell in love with a tortured man, <b>Erik “Ripper” Jacobs</b> who loved her more than his scarred heart dared to admit.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762925.png" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Danny, the daughter of the President of Hell’s Horsemen Motorcycle Club was supposed to get away of the club and the violence. She was to be something more. But happiness isn't in the achievements we make. It's in the details. In your father's smiling eyes, your brother's arms, on your man's bike...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395955ra/762926.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ripper, Sergeant and Brother wasn't supposed to fall for his Prez' Daughter. Scarred, tortured, bitter and older he has no right to Danny but heart wants what the heart wants and when life intervenes you have to fight tooth and nail and be brave enough to go against anything that stands in your way.<br><br><b>
  <i>“We were doomed from the start, weren’t we, baby?”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762927.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They weren't ready to make a stand and fight. To defy all odds and the Motorcycle Club's rules. To face their past and hope for future, together. So they left. Ripper away to fight his demons and Danny withdrew inside her head to fight her dreams, making mistake upon mistake until life came full circle and they are one last chance and one wrong move away of the end. Happiness or doom? It's in their hands to claim. Will they risk the brotherhood, themselves and loved ones, their homes and lives to be together again?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762928._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This also the story of <b>Deuce and Eva</b>, we all felt was left incomplete in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16109563.Undeniable__Undeniable___1_" title="Undeniable (Undeniable, #1) by Madeline Sheehan" rel="nofollow noopener">Undeniable</a>. And if you think that they lived happily ever after, you are gonna get heartbroken....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395955ra/762929.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They are broken. In pieces so small that just like sand, are slipping through their fingers and drifting apart. Frankie managed what everybody else tried and failed. To destroy them. They can't move on, because in their heads they are still in that hellish room, Eva getting raped and Deuce chained to the radiator witnessing the woman he loves be abused by her ex-husband. They have to start all over again, forgive and forget, because if they both know something for certain, is that they live to love each other...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762930.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>An amazing series about unconventional love and undeniable passion. A glimpse in a world ruled by bastards, p*ssies and old ladies. Murderers and criminals. Feelings and emotions clogged by the smell of gasoline, leather and sweat. Life on the other side of the tracks where women must be stronger than men and men don't claim to be heroes. Danny and Ripper's story is unbeautifully perfect but it's theirs and they can do whatever they f*cking want with it...<br><br><b>
  <i>“No sooner met but they looked, no sooner looked but they loved, no sooner loved but they sighed, no sooner sighed but they asked one another the reason, no sooner knew the reason but they sought the remedy…” —William Shakespeare</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762931.jpg" width="400" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b>I can't get this pic out of my head, every time I think of these books...</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Life goes on. If there is nothing else in this world you can count on, you can count on that. Life will go on. With or without you. Before you, after you, all around you, life has always done just that. Gone on.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395955ra/762932.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Life can be so unbeautiful... Work it, seize it, own it!<i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762933.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I am addicted and craving for more, can't wait for Cage and Tegen's story!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395955i/762934._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My feelings upon the book's release:<br><i>4/27/2013 UPDATE: YAAAAYY! IT'S OUT!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395955ra/762935.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i></i></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="12906822705842289124" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
