<div id="review_452461969" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/452461969" />
    <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4402779-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1375835531p2/4402779.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/452461969?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/4402779-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer452461969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13529145786892255107">What the hell did I just read you may wonder? <br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_mbfv22c0FK1rwrt0y_zpsb44d4045.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765991.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mbfv22c0FK1rwrt0y_zpsb44d4045.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Well sit down and cross your legs ladies and gentleman because when you hear about Unbeautifully by Madeline Sheehan, you run the risk of having your panties (or manties) run off into a lust filled abyss of awesomeness. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_m13nvgovfn1r1denq_zps94831a90.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765992.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_m13nvgovfn1r1denq_zps94831a90.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Last year I had the pleasure of reading book one of Sheehan's motorcycle club series promptly named, Undeniable. (Fun fact it was supposed to be a stand alone, but being that Madeline is a fucking Goddess of EPIC proportions s</span>
  <span id="freeText13529145786892255107" style="display:none">What the hell did I just read you may wonder? <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_mbfv22c0FK1rwrt0y_zpsb44d4045.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765991.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mbfv22c0FK1rwrt0y_zpsb44d4045.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Well sit down and cross your legs ladies and gentleman because when you hear about Unbeautifully by Madeline Sheehan, you run the risk of having your panties (or manties) run off into a lust filled abyss of awesomeness. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_m13nvgovfn1r1denq_zps94831a90.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765992.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m13nvgovfn1r1denq_zps94831a90.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Last year I had the pleasure of reading book one of Sheehan's motorcycle club series promptly named, Undeniable. (Fun fact it was supposed to be a stand alone, but being that Madeline is a fucking Goddess of EPIC proportions she wrote another book for her fans AND recently told us that she will be adding another THREE, yes THREE books to the line up. This bitch is my hero. For real.)<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_mc21wwGPoX1rq65rlo1_500_zps21262c7b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765993.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mc21wwGPoX1rq65rlo1_500_zps21262c7b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Undeniable threw me into a world of lust, hurt, pain, wonder, hatred, belly drops from hell, and most importantly a real taste of the fucked up, but totally legit love story of Deuce and Eva. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_m4wq14toy91rqfhi2o1_400_zps2ffd941f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765994.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m4wq14toy91rqfhi2o1_400_zps2ffd941f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That book ruined me. <br><br>There were parts where I just knew I was going to stroke out, or throw up all of my insides. Madeline has a way of getting under your skin to secretly rip your fucking heart out, while calmly keeping your punk ass alive, whilst your bloody, traitor of a heart erratically beats in her tortuous grasp. Then she holds your heart captive until SHE is ready to let you go, and even after that bitch ass heart is back in its place you're still fucked up in the head from the royal mind fuck that just slapped you in the puss. Curtiously delivered by those fucking ingenious digits of hers which spout this fucked up beautiful mess of a book out on to her computer screen. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_m0d8yhFLFR1qihw4io1_500_large_zps4db99dd8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765995.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m0d8yhFLFR1qihw4io1_500_large_zps4db99dd8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yes I feel that strongly about these books. That's how you know that your shit is REAL. Undeniable put me into the biggest book funk I've had to date because I couldn't REEL IT IN. Deuce and Eva have been on my brain for months, then finally....oh lord sweet baby jesus FINALLY Madeline released Unbeautifully early. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_lj9okiHLQP1qixleeo1_250_zps67fdb4a4.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765996.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lj9okiHLQP1qixleeo1_250_zps67fdb4a4.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ladies and Gentlemen, I found God and her name is Madeline Sheehan. We need a statue or something erected in this woman's honor because yet again she has released some beauty into this world that no one else can do. <br><br>Unbeautifully is the story of Danny (Deuce's baby girl from Undeniable) and the scarred bad boy, Ripper. <br><br>I will admit, I didn't think I'd be as hooked on Danny and Ripper as I was Deuce and Eva, but once again Madeline proved me wrong. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/omgwtf_zps2b8007a2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765997.gif" alt=" photo omgwtf_zps2b8007a2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Unbeautifully has something for everyone. There are swoon moments, hot moments, OMFG TAKE ME NOW moments, youfuckingbastardhowcouldyou moments, laugh your ass off moments, and the most important to me, the "ah ha" moments. Danny's transformation from Undeniable to the end of Unbeautifully is something only an extremely skilled writer could pull off. It was nothing short of amazing and (to me) inspiring as hell.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_mgjcw1OJaa1rifv07o1_500_large_zpsbe22426c.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>If you've read Undeniable, you already know that our boy Frankie did one hell of a number on Ripper. Ripper is scarred pretty bad, but Danny sees past that shit and loves him for who he is on the inside and not the shit that's on the outside. I was not expecting that from an 18 barbie-esq girl who wore pink and bling twenty-four seven. <br><br>Sheehan weaves the pieces together flawlessly to where you feel the pain and turmoil that Frankie caused during his crazy escapades during Undeniable. He fucked everyone up and even after he's long gone he is still causing all sorts of pain for a number of people. Unbeautifully picks up where Undeniable left off and you are given a taste of the hurt that everyone is feeling and why the characters are acting the way they are.<br><br>Danny is lonely and down on life. Ripper provides her with a night of letting go and being free of all of the worries in her life. Yeah it might have not been the greatest of ideas, but I loved it! I think I turned five shades of red when I read some of the lines that he said to her during THAT scene at the lake.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_mfzav1hGjk1rw1o51o1_500_zps5f390e47.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/765999.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mfzav1hGjk1rw1o51o1_500_zps5f390e47.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh lawd jeebus it's an orgasm!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/couple-kiss-passion-Favimcom-294732_large_zps8c61aac2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/766000.gif" alt=" photo couple-kiss-passion-Favimcom-294732_large_zps8c61aac2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Reel it in, Brandi. Ok where was I? Oh right, from that night forward we are taken on a roller coaster ride of emotions. Some of which are from Deuce and Eva's point of view because after what happened to them in Undeniable, shit didn't automatically fix itself. It was raw and it was real. Like I've said a million times before Madeline can do no wrong with her characters. I have mad respect for this woman and her brutal honestly about shit that most people would gloss over and tie up with a pretty bow. <br><br>Fuck that she said, here let me crush your soul and laugh in your face while I hang it over your head that they will in fact get over this shitty ass hump in life and be stronger than ever. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/we-not-worthy_zpsacb3f260.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/766001.gif" alt=" photo we-not-worthy_zpsacb3f260.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She's twisted like that, but I wouldn't have it any other way! Unbeautifully was just as good, if not better than Undeniable. I'm more than ever invested in this serious and I can.not.wait. until the next book which is going to be Cage and Teegan's story. That one is going to blow the roof off of the fucking house!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/tumblr_m6f13pbekP1rziwwco2_500_zpsf192c593.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397113ra/766002.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m6f13pbekP1rziwwco2_500_zpsf192c593.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Thank you Madeline AGAIN for sharing your world with us. You're the coolest bitch I know. #DeuceBabe4life!<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/brandidid1/media/7zJHR_zps2d75afd5.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer467238343" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2550492789402952382">*ARC given to blog for honest review*<br/><br/>5+++ MOTHER FUCKING <b> “Beautiful Girl” </b> Kisses!!!<br/><br/><b> *WARNING* This review will have profanity…I am about to go off on one of the best books I have read this year, possibly ever in my life and if you don’t like the word “fuck”…just stop now. :-) Oh and as usual, I will babble </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399323ra/772639.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><i> ‘Fuck. Jesus fucking fuck.’</i>….can I just say that I have been waiting for UnBeautifully since the second I finished UnDeniable. Why, might you ask? Because…these characters crawl into your b</span>
  <span id="freeText2550492789402952382" style="display:none">*ARC given to blog for honest review*<br><br>5+++ MOTHER FUCKING <b> “Beautiful Girl” </b> Kisses!!!<br><br><b> *WARNING* This review will have profanity…I am about to go off on one of the best books I have read this year, possibly ever in my life and if you don’t like the word “fuck”…just stop now. :-) Oh and as usual, I will babble </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399323ra/772639.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i> ‘Fuck. Jesus fucking fuck.’</i>….can I just say that I have been waiting for UnBeautifully since the second I finished UnDeniable. Why, might you ask? Because…these characters crawl into your brain, fuck you up in the best way possible and then pop a squat for the long haul, never letting go and you <b> love </b> it. You <b> want</b> it. You <b>beg</b> for it and <b>crave</b> it. Don’t ask me how Madleine does it, she has magic jedi powers or some shit. <br><br><b> “Baby,” he said, “listen to me. I ain’t beautiful, you are. You’re so damn beautiful you got it spillin’ out all over the place, blindin’ you into thinkin’ I’m beautiful when I ain’t. Farthest thing from it.” </b><br><br>So…if you haven’t read UnDeniable, A.) What the fuck is wrong with you? B.) Stop whatever your doing and read it right fucking now? And C.) Don’t even crack open UnBeautifully until you do. First of all, let me address the prologue…the first 17 lines of this book, all highlighted. Because it’s beautifully written, profound and the straight up fucking truth hitting you in the face. It stole my breath, brought tears to my eyes and at that point I knew I was going to love this book. Those 17 lines solidified it for me.<br><br><b> “Jesus,” he whispered, running his thumb along my mouth, tugging it open, gently stroking my bottom lip. “Why can’t I say no to you?” </b><br><br>UnB picks up where UnD left off, seamlessly, you jump right back into the story of the Hell’s Horsemen Motorcycle Club. This time around, we start off with Danny’s POV. Danielle Elizabeth West…18 and Deuce’s eldest daughter, she’s an angel among devil’s and despite her father being the president of a motorcycle gang, she’s a good girl that’s got her head on straight. Until life smacks her in the face.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399323i/772640.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> ‘That’s how this shit was with Danny.<br>It was an accident, a mistake, it was the wrong place at the wrong time kind of shit that had quickly turned into a catastrophe of epic proportions.<br>If she’d just been pussy, if he’d fucked her at the lake then forgotten about it…<br>But Danny was different.<br>A game changer.<br>She wasn’t pussy, she was damned beautiful and everything he’d ever wanted in a woman but hadn’t realized until he held her in his arms.<br>She was the reason his world was about to shatter again.’ </b><br><br>Erik “Ripper” Jacobs…oh my sweet baby JESUS this man. He’s dark. He’s twisted. He’s scared, on the inside and out. But he’s so fuckin beautiful. At 32 his lived a life with more pain and suffering, just the thought of it makes my eyes water. He’s a bad ass don’t get me wrong but even through his imperfections, he’s perfect. I swooned over Deuce, hard, but Ripper held my heart in his hand. <br><br><b> ‘He was an incredibly beautiful man. The scars just forced you to look a little harder to see what was still there, and what was still there was the squared, strong, bone structure of a Greek god, the heavily muscled stature of a boxer, and a deviously sexy smile.’ </b><br><br>They first meet when Danny is 3 and Ripper is 17 <i>‘at a bike rally while on a run through San Antonio.’</i> This isn’t crucial information, I just love it cause I’m from San Antonio…and fuck yeah, they met in my hometown :-) (ha…I’m a dork!) Another thing is the age difference, let’s just building a big fucking bridge and get over it right about now…14 years, oh wow, so big (I wish I had a sarcastic emoticon I could insert here…) Alright, everyone over that fact? Good…we can move on.<br><br><b> ‘The things this man made me feel just by speaking was unreal. At times I wanted to weep from the sheer sensation of never before experienced feelings that I knew had already wrecked me for any other man.’ </b><br><br>I was all set and ready for Danny and Ripper, and then….Madeline decided to surprise me. You don’t just get Danny and Ripper’s POV….*suspenseful pause* We get Deuce and Eva!!!! YAY!!!!! OMG best surprise ever! So you’ve got four different POV’s, two different couples stories – there are many opportunities for things to get confusing, flow to get a little messy – nope. Doesn’t happen. I promise you it’s seamless and effortless. I knew everything between Eva and Deuce wasn’t ‘perfect’ after the shit storm that happened in UnD, but Lord have mercy. I cried…a lot. They both were hurting so bad and there is not one fucking thing you can do about it besides hold on and just know in the back of your mind everything is okay in the end.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399323ra/772641.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b> ‘Because once you had a taste of a good woman, suddenly nothing else mattered but her.<br>Nothing.’ </b><br><br>So back to Danny and Ripper. God I love these two. They ‘shouldn’t be together’ but they can’t stay away, which makes me want them to be together more. And if the fact that they couldn’t be open with their relationship wasn’t enough to kill me things kept getting worse…and worse, until I was in the fetal position just crying my eyes out. I hurt for them. Physically…Emotionally…that’s what Madeline Sheehan did to me with her writing.<br><br><b> ‘I was a wreck, my life was a wreck, everything was just…wrong.<br>Irreparable.<br>And all I could think about was Ripper.’ </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399323ra/772642.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alright so it wasn’t all doom and gloom and sadness – there were <b>SO</b> many times where I was laughing so hard I couldn’t breathe. Kami and Cox are sheer brilliance on paper…and I have two words that will forever make me think of them and crack up…<i> ‘American Indian’ </i>. I loved seeing more of characters we were introduced to in UnD, but getting a better glimpse of in UnB. I loved that there was a 3 paragraph comparison of orgasms to a rainy day and rainstorm (just trust me, it’s genius), I loved the word <i>’sexalicious’</i> was used, and of course…being a classic dirty book whore, I <b>loved</b> all the sex. Hot. Mind Blowing. Amazing. Sex. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399323ra/772643.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> But the best thing in the book…was a line, that will always mean so much more to me than I can express…<i> ‘Don’t let the lack of mustache fool ya, baby,” he said, grinning. “I’m always down for a gang bang.” </i> Just typing those words brings joy to my heart that I can’t even put into words. Even though I was gutted and wrecked through so much, the ending pulled me through and I couldn’t be happier. The epilogue was magical…perfect…loved it. *sigh*<br><br><b> ‘No, he didn’t care about anything else in the world except for his woman, the sweetest kid he’d ever met, the smartest too, a kid who’d turned into the sexiest woman he’d ever seen. A woman who didn’t just love with her whole heart but with her body and soul. A woman who time and time again, brought him to his fucking knees, had him prayer to a god he didn’t believe in just so he could keep her by his side.<br>A woman whose motherfucking smile made the world and his life seem somewhat livable. Even worth it sometimes.’ </b><br><br>I got the same feelings with UnB as I did in UnD, but I was more prepared for them this time around. I welcomed them with open arms. In UnD I struggled with the fact that I was liking a book that by ‘society’s’ standards, I prolly shouldn’t like – but with UnB, I straight up didn’t give a fuck. I LOVE that this book is so different, I want that in a book. I want something that breaks the mold, challenges me and still makes me love the shit out of it, that’s fucking awesome. This book is not fucking sunshine and roses…if you’re looking for that, you’re in the wrong book. But that doesn’t mean it isn’t a beautiful fuckin story about real and raw people that are flawed and yet perfect all in the same breath.<br><br><b> “Ripper, I’ve always been yours.” </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399323i/772644.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To say I am unapologetically, completely and 100% certifiably in love with Madeline’s brain and all the genius that comes out of it is putting it mildly. I want to live, breathe and exist in the world she has created. And I also want Cage’s story…<b>now</b>. :-)</span>

<div id="review_444111691" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/444111691" />
    <a title="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa"><img alt="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557708088p2/3531683.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/444111691?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" href="/user/show/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa">Spoiler Whore-Momoa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa?shelf=madeline-sheehan">madeline-sheehan</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer444111691" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4658758984351763158">4.5 stars <br/><br/>I'm gonna punish Ms. Sheehan and not give her that .5 star cause after I savored the book, it left me wanting more. So much more more more.<br/><br/>If you're a hater, guess what hater, you'll be hating.<br/><br/>If you're a lover...be prepared. Lock yourself into a room, get comfortable, have a drink by your side, shut off your phone, put a do not disturb sign on the door cause you are gonna be on one helluva ride.<br/><br/>Here are 6 easy steps before, during and after you get into Unbeautifully.<br/><br/>1. Breathe In, Br</span>
  <span id="freeText4658758984351763158" style="display:none">4.5 stars <br /><br />I'm gonna punish Ms. Sheehan and not give her that .5 star cause after I savored the book, it left me wanting more. So much more more more.<br /><br />If you're a hater, guess what hater, you'll be hating.<br /><br />If you're a lover...be prepared. Lock yourself into a room, get comfortable, have a drink by your side, shut off your phone, put a do not disturb sign on the door cause you are gonna be on one helluva ride.<br /><br />Here are 6 easy steps before, during and after you get into Unbeautifully.<br /><br />1. Breathe In, Breathe Out<br /><br />2. Take your time reading the book. Don't rush yourself.<br /><br />3. Breathe In, Breathe Out<br /><br />4. Give yourself permission to show your emotions while reading the story. Just don't do anything to get yourself in trouble.<br /><br />5. Breathe In, Breathe Out<br /><br />6. Reread cause it will be a while till we get Unattainable(which I can't freakin wait for, Mad love for Teagan)<br /><br />I'm not gonna spoil anything even if that's my name but I will say this, Fuckin A(while raising fist in air) can Madeline write a story. <br /><br />*<br /><br />*<br /><br />*<br /><br />*<br /><br />Shit, this is hard to write without giving spoilers so here are little clues from the story...<br /><br />*Some demons can take a long time to conquer <br /><br />*Memories are not forgotten<br /><br />*Assholes are assholes<br /><br />*Love is a bitch<br /><br />*The ripple effect is huge in this story<br /><br />*Sex, yep it's in there and yep it's pretty damn hot<br /><br /><br />There are some of these type of moments:<br /><br />*Fuck me, I didn't see <b>THAT</b> coming!<br /><br />*Laugh Out Loud...there are plenty of those<br /><br />*Don't do it Asshole!!! <br /><br />*Fuck me, he did it<br /><br />*Oh, bitch is gonna get it now<br /><br /><br />These are not good guys except for Blue, whatever he's done, he's forgiven and ZZ(sigh). You fuck with them or their families, you'll get their wrath. There was a scene that made me not like the horsemen too much. It's part of their way, not usually, but I visually saw it even if it didn't go into details. You know what happened. <br /><br />Well that's all I got. Don't compare Madeline to any author out there. She's on a shelf of her own.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4658758984351763158" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Kudos to Ms Sheehan for never failing us. <br/><br/>This story picks up right after the Epilogue of Undeniable but then scoots back three years.....building you back up to present time. </a><br><br>Unbeautifully was literally everything biker awesome that Undeniable was. Kudos to Ms Sheehan for never failing us. <br><br>This story picks up right after the Epilogue of Undeniable but then scoots back three years.....building you back up to present time. It's the story of Danny, Duece's daughter and Ripper, Master at Arms of the Hell's Horsemen MC Club. He's over a decade older than Danny, his face and torso horribly scarred from the assault by Frankie in Undeniable, and he's got a glass eye.....but he's still beautiful in Danny's eyes.<br><br>Everything changes for these two when Ripper shows up at Danny's prom to pick her up. Except she doesn't want to go home. Danny asks for him to put brotherhood aside....to make love to her. Their tumultuous love story begins from there. <br><br>The relationship between these two starts out as complete, unbridled lust- they physically cannot get enough of each other. They fuck, fuck, and top it off with a fuck....<br><br><b> “He looked down at his flaccid cock. "Congratulations," he said. "You've just fucked yourself to death</b><br><br>It's angsty...he's a brother, her father would kill him if he knew he was tapping Danny. Things have to remain quiet. But their combustible attraction cannot be denied....it won't take long until those stolen private moments, looks shared across the room start to uncover the truth. Ripper is torn between brotherhood loyalty to the Horsemen and his love for Danny. Not to mention he likely won't survive the wrath of Deuce once he finds out. <br><br> <b> "I wanna rip you the fuck open," he said, breathing harder as his thrusts became brutal.<br> "I want all of me inside of you, not just my fucking cock, baby, but all of me."</b><br><br>I loved that this book had several stories in one. We got to see Deuce and Eva and their struggles post Frankie madness. How they work through their problems to an eventual happily ever after. We get the continuing saga of Jace, Dorothy, and Hawk (looking forward to their story in Undeniable #4). Cage (Danny's man-whore brother) and Tegan have a set-up for their story in Undeniable #3. ZZ..... well, no spoilers here but I want to see a HEA for this sweetie (he's Undeniable #5). I do have to say my favorite couple is Cox and Kami. They had me laughting out loud. She has him "by the balls" and it's refreshing to hear her banter, calling him a dumb Mexican, Cuban....everything BUT Puerto Rican. Cox was such a loyal good friend to Ripper- he deserved an Allison shout-out. This is a great series filled with a family of rough, dirty, illegal shit going-on but loyalty till the end. It is not for the faint at heart. There's rape, murder, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[abortion <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>and everything dark but I still can't get enough of the Horsemen crew and their old ladies.<br><br>Loved Ripper. He's all scarred and knows he doesn't deserve Danny but he tried to walk away...he just kept getting drawn back. Nobody will have her. She's his lady. She's gonna be on the back of his bike....but he may be "put to ground" by her father before that dream comes to play..... But he's gonna try. <br><br>Loved Danny. She was young but she was tough. Ripper tore her heart. She did things she'd regret in its wake but her heart always belonged to him. She tried life outside of Ripper.... And failed. <br><br>It may not be philosophical and flowery, but Danny dear, no truer words have ever been said.......<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_443721839" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/443721839" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/443721839?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer443721839" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14873077437999747192">Heed this well: <br/><br/><i>
  <b>"Warning: This is not a story about fate or destiny. This is a story about pain, sorrow, and suffering."</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791513i/551247._SX540_.png' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Truer words have not be spoken. As with the first book, <i>Undeniable</i>, this book is dark and gritty. The author usually takes you to that extreme...almost the worst case scenario. That doesn't mean there aren't happy and sweet times, it just means they are far and few between. <br/><br/>I'm just going to start with my biggest complaint and it's that I feel cheated! While I wasn't sure h</span>
  <span id="freeText14873077437999747192" style="display:none">Heed this well: <br><br><i>
  <b>"Warning: This is not a story about fate or destiny. This is a story about pain, sorrow, and suffering."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791513i/551247._SX540_.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Truer words have not be spoken. As with the first book, <i>Undeniable</i>, this book is dark and gritty. The author usually takes you to that extreme...almost the worst case scenario. That doesn't mean there aren't happy and sweet times, it just means they are far and few between. <br><br>I'm just going to start with my biggest complaint and it's that I feel cheated! While I wasn't sure how much I would like Ripper and Danny's story...I still wanted to read <i>their</i> story but what we got was half a story...if that. And while I'm not really complaining (<i>not really</i>!), I wasn't expecting almost half the book to be about Deuce and Eva. <br><br>I wanted <b>more</b> Ripper and Danny...heck, I WANT more Ripper and Danny. I feel like we barely got a taste and it's over. My only consolation is that if <i>Unattainable</i> follows the pattern, we'll get more Ripper and Danny in that book. Then I'll get to be mad about Cage and Tegen!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791513i/551248.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=nSz16ngdsG0" rel="nofollow noopener">This</a>
  </i>
</b>...is their song! ♥ <br><br>As far as Deuce and Eva are concerned, that killed me. I didn't want to read any more heartache about those two. And I certainly didn't want to read about what Deuce attempted to do....<i>really??!!</i> Could you imagine if Eva did that!! (Yes, Deuce is still a douchebag!) But...I understand how their relationship affected their family and consequently Danny. I mentioned in my review for <i>Undeniable</i> that I hope Deuce gets what's coming to him and he did...some. But I kind of forgive him a little, <i>just a little</i>, after he said this: <br><br><i>
  <b>"But Jesus, Danny, who am I to be judgin’ anyone? Made my fair share of mistakes too. I spent too much time wantin’ a woman I kept lettin’ get away, and I don’t want that for you.”</b>
</i><br><br>Back to Danny and Ripper...I LOVE them!! Well, I did for the first fifty percent. How Ripper was with her was perfect...even if he was freaking out about Deuce. He was sooo loving that even I forgot about his scars...<br><br><i>
  <b>“All scars tell a story, beautiful girl,” he said, releasing me to trace the marks on my stomach.[...] <br><br>“And mine,” he said softly, grabbing my hand, trailing my palm across his cheek and then his chest. “Tell the story of how I found you.”</b>
</i><br><br>Of course, things have to get effed up...no, not effed up, more like BLOWN ALL TO HELL!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/551249.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Danny,” he said, glancing over his shoulder. “Shit just got real, baby.”</i>
</b><br><br>I really get what Ripper was doing to try to forget Danny but the way he left? My heart went out to Danny but then, of course, she has to do something unforgivable. (Wow...that was a bit intense!) The crazy part about all this is this kind of stuff goes on every day in the real world so why is it so shocking? <br><br>The interesting thing about this book is that all the different dramas had a trickle down effect. A lot of the old characters and some new ones were involved with each drama and most of them were left open ended. The fantastic thing is that MS will be writing more stories about those characters. <br><br>The book is really emotional. Again, with all the other dramas and especially with Danny and Ripper. One of my favorite parts is how they spoke to each other "silently". I LOVED that...especially the one at the end with Mama Vi. Ughhh...I just wanted more of them! I can't say that enough.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791513i/551246.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And speaking of Mama Vi...what happened with her? I was repulsed. Remember those worse case scenarios...well, this is one of them. Bad Dirty and Tap, BAD!! <br><br>Of course, the epilogue was wonderful and it was sorely needed. This book was rough and while it didn't have the shock value the first book had, there were still scenes that were hard to read. Thankfully, we didn't have to go through something happening with Ripper and someone else in the kitchen! <br><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♥ “Baby,” he said gruffly. “Man like me got no business with a girl like you. You’re nothin’ but f*ckin’ beauty and I’m a whole lot of f*ckin’ ugly who’s already halfway to hell.”<br><br>♦ "Maybe this was how his miserable life was finally going to end: death by p*ssy." (LMAO!) <br><br>♥ "He didn’t just want to f*ck her, he didn’t just want her in his bed… <br><br><i>He wanted her on the back of his bike.</i>"<br><br>♥ "Ripper was my rainstorm, my skin-drenching frenzy, where you couldn’t tell right from left, where all you could feel was the phenomenon exploding throughout your body, feverishly burning through you even as it pleasurably cooled."</span>
  <a data-text-id="14873077437999747192" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_612908012" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/612908012" />
    <a title="Mo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11856352-mo"><img alt="Mo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371247812p2/11856352.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/612908012?book_show_action=true">May 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer612908012" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12662927163650746926">4.5 Stars....<br/><br/><br/><u>… but fuck, brother, you have been with me for eighteen loyal years now and that means you’re family.</u><br/><br/>Yep, this book was about family and when I started it I thought I was with this family …..<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421217i/836522.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It was all the names, Jim-Bob, Ripper, John-Boy, Digger, Tick, Elizabeth, Hawk, Cage, Mary-Ellen, Grandma, Pop, Preacher …. I was confused.<br/><br/>BUT, I soon realized I was not on Walton Mountain, No Siree – this was a much darker place….<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387362158i/7583909._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>"I don’t believe in fate. I firmly believe that life is what you </b></span>
  <span id="freeText12662927163650746926" style="display:none">4.5 Stars....<br><br><br><u>… but fuck, brother, you have been with me for eighteen loyal years now and that means you’re family.</u><br><br>Yep, this book was about family and when I started it I thought I was with this family …..<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421217i/836522.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was all the names, Jim-Bob, Ripper, John-Boy, Digger, Tick, Elizabeth, Hawk, Cage, Mary-Ellen, Grandma, Pop, Preacher …. I was confused.<br><br>BUT, I soon realized I was not on Walton Mountain, No Siree – this was a much darker place….<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387362158i/7583909._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>"I don’t believe in fate. I firmly believe that life is what you make of it, that life will react to your actions, and that your final destination has nothing to do with destiny but instead everything to do with the choices you make along the way.<br>With one exception.<br>Love.<br>There are not rules when it comes to love.<br>Love is not a reaction or an action; it is not a destiny or a choice.<br>Love is a feeling, a real, raw and unscripted emotion so sensationally pure, unable to dull even under the strain of a world against it, strong enough to heal the broken and warm even the coldest of hearts.<br>Innate.<br>Unavoidable.<br><i>Undeniable."</i></b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379791513i/551246.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380973837i/3619980.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399054ra/771819.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380973837i/3619981.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>"He felt the walls of his world start to shake and the bricks began to fall … one-by one until it was a free-for-all and suddenly he could breathe again when he hadn’t even realized he’d been holding his breath. Breath he’d been holding for the last five years."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421217i/836523.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> "HE WANTED HER ON THE BACK OF HIS BIKE …."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379768519i/268576._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380973838i/3619982._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>"If Ripper had learned anything in his thirty-something years of life, it was that dark roads only get darker if you stay on them, and his road was pretty damn dark."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421217i/836524.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Aw, Danny… don’t cry..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380973838i/3619983.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Aw, Cage, gotta love a …<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380973838i/3619984._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>"This is what big brothers are fuckin’ here for….. to pick their little sisters up when they fall the fuck down."</b><br><br><br><br><i>" This wasn’t love. It was hate. And love.<br>That fine line had been destroyed.<br>Mutilated." </i><br><br><br><b>"FUCK YOU! he roared as his fist shot out. The mirror shattered on impact.<br>Shattered.<br>Just like his fucking life."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421217i/836525._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380973838i/3619985.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"… And he kissed her.<br>And kissed her.<br>Fucking kissed her.<br>Kissed the fucking shit out of her.<br>Kissed her the way he’d been wanting to kiss her since he’d left her.<br>“Fuck,” he muttered in between kisses. Suffocating, nearly violent kisses that were growing harder, even more demanding."</b><br><br>OH, MY, RIPPER!<br><br><b>"Jesus. Why couldn’t he had had boys? All boys. Little fucking shits like Cage. A whole slew of ‘em he could throw condoms at and be done with it."</b><br><br>LOL, Deuce, know what you mean – not sure I could have handled a daughter myself!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421217i/836526._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><b>"He didn’t hate me. He didn’t even hate Ripper. He wasn’t even mad. He was disappointed. I had <i>disappointed</i> him.<br>It was infinitely worse. "</b><br><br>Yep, worst feeling ever, the thought that you had disappointed your parents!<br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"Life may not always go the way you’d planned, you may not have the perfect family, you may not be the most beautiful, but that doesn’t mean you can’t make the best of what you do have. My father wasn’t perfect, far from it. He’s made a lot of mistakes and I had no doubt he was going to make a lot more. But he was mine and I wouldn’t trade him for the world."</i>
</b><br><br>I really loved catching up with Deuce and Eva in this book …<br><br><br>…. And just when I thought everything was gliding towards a nice, happy ending… guess who the fuck shows up???<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421217i/836527.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I had to live.<br>I had to see him.<br>I had to tell him I loved him.<br>I had to live. "</b><br><br><br>Well, it all kinda ended suddenly after SHE showed up… but I didn't mind 'cos my head was spinning from all that went on and trying to remember who was who.<br><br>Yes, it is gritty, violent, the language is dreadful but I did like it.<br><br>Yes, It is <s>Digger</s> Ripper and Danny’s story but it is also the story of Deuce and Eva… so kinda like two for the price of one!<br>Enjoy it.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I seriously did not like the intimation of a “gang-bang” with Vi, really don’t think that was necessary. See deep down I am a prude and a nice person…. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421217ra/836528.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380973838i/3619987._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380973838i/3619988._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380973838i/3619989.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/551269436" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/551269436?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer551269436" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3860889587226679667"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809762._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809763._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>(^^ add scars!)<br/><br/>I abso-fucking-lutely <b>love</b> these books!!! And <i>Unbeautifully</i> delivered to the nth degree!<br/><br/><b>Five Rip-Roaring, Motherfucking, Unbeautiful Stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809764.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I feel the need to include a little warning in my reviews of Madeline's books, to those who aren't familiar with the <i>Undeniable</i> series.<br/>If you are a fan of fluffy romance, chick lit and opposed to bad language, violence and other unmentionables, these books will not be for you. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809765.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Madeline holds nothing back in her books. Think gang rape, murder, '</span>
  <span id="freeText3860889587226679667" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809762._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809763._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(^^ add scars!)<br><br>I abso-fucking-lutely <b>love</b> these books!!! And <i>Unbeautifully</i> delivered to the nth degree!<br><br><b>Five Rip-Roaring, Motherfucking, Unbeautiful Stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809764.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I feel the need to include a little warning in my reviews of Madeline's books, to those who aren't familiar with the <i>Undeniable</i> series.<br>If you are a fan of fluffy romance, chick lit and opposed to bad language, violence and other unmentionables, these books will not be for you. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809765.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Madeline holds nothing back in her books. Think gang rape, murder, 'fuck' in every sentence and a whole lot more. I totally get that this won't be for everybody, but personally, it totally fascinates me and I can't get enough of them.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>After all the shit they'd gone through - the pain, the loss, the heartache, the straight up evil brutality that made them question everything they'd thought to be true and had nearly driven them apart for good - he knew he'd do anything for her. Steal anything, kill anyone, be anyone.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I've always had a real morbid fascination with dark, sociological, criminal underworld kinds of stories, so for me, this hits every spot. But it's certainly not everyone's bag. So I would strongly advise you not to read these books if you don't think you can cope with the unconventional, gritty, violent, raw content.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Love is a feeling, a real, raw, and unscripted emotion so sensationally pure, unable to dull even under the strain of a world against it, strong enough to heal the broken and warm even the coldest of hearts.<br>Innate.<br>Unavoidable.<br>Undeniable.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Ok, that said, I could read these books alllll day long! <br><br>I love the dialogue, the flow, the characters, the ease at which the author tells the story, the alternating POVs and between first and third person. All of it. It just works! And then some. It's one of those you'll be reading while you're cooking/drying your hair/making the coffee. It's one of those books that will make you great at doing everything one handed.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I love her," he rasped, his eyes on Danny. "You want me to beg, I'll fuckin' beg. I'll do whatever I gotta do if it means she keeps breathin'."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The characters; I feel like I know them all so well. Madeline Sheehan does a fantastic job of building a whole network of detailed, life-like characters.<br><br>I loved that Eva and Deuce's story continued within <i>Unbeautifully</i>. It was great to have those gaps filled in and read more of them.<br><br>And Ripper and Danny's story was gripping.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809766._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was fast paced, hot and heavy, original and real! A story where opposites attract and beautiful is discovered in a whole heap of fugly!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>He didn't just want to fuck her, he didn't just want her in his bed...<br>He wanted her on the back of his bike.<br>Yeah, he wanted to lay claim to Danielle West, ink his name on her body and slap an old lady patch on her ass. And worse, he wanted the world to know it.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>These are the characters that you know you should hate, but can't help but love. These aggressive, trigger-happy, rebellious, can't-keep-their-dick-in-their-pants, foul mouthed, badass bikers, who work their way straight into your heart. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I'm tryin' to figure out whether I'm gonna slap some sense into you or fuck the shit outta you."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I'd let any one of 'em put me on the back of their bikes!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411925i/809767._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732852i/8051744._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389732852i/8051745._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBookBlog">https://www.facebook.com/SmittensBook...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14593217530999828501">***I recieved this ARC in return for an honest review***<br/><br/>This review can also be found at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com' rel='nofollow noopener'> www.mysecretromancebookreviews.com </a><br/><br/><br/><i> “No sooner met but they looked,<br/>No sooner looked but they loved,<br/>No sooner loved but they sighed,<br/>No sooner sighed but they<br/>Asked one another the reason,<br/>No sooner knew the reason<br/>But they sought the remedy…”</i><br/> <br/>-William Shakespeare <br/><br/><br/><i> I don’t believe in fate. I firmly believe that life is what you make of it, that life will react to your actions and that your final destination has </i></span>
  <span id="freeText14593217530999828501" style="display:none">***I recieved this ARC in return for an honest review***<br /><br />This review can also be found at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com" rel="nofollow noopener"> www.mysecretromancebookreviews.com </a><br /><br /><br /><i> “No sooner met but they looked,<br />No sooner looked but they loved,<br />No sooner loved but they sighed,<br />No sooner sighed but they<br />Asked one another the reason,<br />No sooner knew the reason<br />But they sought the remedy…”</i><br /> <br />-William Shakespeare <br /><br /><br /><i> I don’t believe in fate. I firmly believe that life is what you make of it, that life will react to your actions and that your final destination has nothing to do with destiny but instead everything to do with the choices you make along the way.<br />With one exception.<br />Love. </i><br />-Madeline Sheehan <i> from UnBeautifully </i><br /><br />Silence. That is all that surrounds me once I finished reading the last page of UnBeautifully because…. <br /><br />1.) It is 2:00a.m. in the fucking morning. <br /><br />2.) My whole being is so damn full of emotions that I fear that if I should cry, shout, run around naked playing the trombone and profess my undying loyalty and love for Madeline in such a sweet vulgar way, that I will be pimping new bracelets which would be provided by the lovely local law enforcements.<br /><br /><b> Wow! Son of a motherless goat that was fanfuckin’ragingcrazyBLOWMYMINDtastic!! (Yes that is all one word!)</b><br /><br />UnBeautifully was Beautifully written and done so perfectly well that I am pronouncing Madeline as a fucking GENUIS! A Beautiful, loving, sexy, crazy, Russian looking, Queen of Vulgaria GENUIS!!<br /><br />I’m not going to go on about the storyline because I truly…TRULY feel like I just can’t do it justice and knowing my fucking luck I will put a spoiler in there and have y’all kicking and probably murdering my ass. So I will say this…<br /><br />UnB picks up where UnD leaves off and if y’all wanted more raw, real, angst, love and heartache then y’all are going to cream y’alls breeches because Mad delivers big time. UnB will have you laughing your fucking ass off, heart bursting with love, heart shattering when *** and *** happens, shocked because *** &amp; *** have something going on, wanting to kick some major ass on ***, crying and hoping that *** &amp; *** will be okay.<br /><br />All the characters are fucking amazing (even the crazy ass character ***. Straight up cray cray!). We not only get Ripper and Danny’s story but others as well. I am so looking forward to Cage and Tegen’s book (is it ready RC?) and I so wish Kami and Cox were real and had their own reality show because I would so watch that shit.<br /><br />If UnDeniable didn’t leave you having biker lust/fever than I can promise you this…you will have it so fucking bad after UnBeautifully. <br /><br />*I am tempted to get Mad’s face tattooed on my back with her name going around my neck. And instead of tears tattooed on my face, I will get mini shanks. One with the initials UFG &amp; the other with RC with a Hello Kitty design.*<br /><br />Until next time…assjuice guzzlers<br /><br />Happy Reading :)<br /><br />Lovingly,<br />UFG!!</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/444866597" />
    <a title="HILLZ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11620952-hillz"><img alt="HILLZ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1549299902p2/11620952.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/444866597?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="HILLZ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="HILLZ" href="/user/show/11620952-hillz">HILLZ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer444866597" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6537727755348617244">LIVE ON AMAZON! <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00CRJNH9I?ie=UTF8&force-full-site=1&ref_=aw_bottom_links'>http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00C...</a><br/><br/>When I first read UnDeniable I thought, now here is a book that is honest, raw and a true page-turner. I honestly didn’t think Madeline could top herself. I mean, if you’ve read UnDeniable, you know what I mean. <b>
  <u>I.WAS.WRONG.</u>
</b><br/><br/>UnBeautifully is the heart wrenching, scarred, frustrating, intense and ultimately <b>BEAUTIFUL</b> story of Danny & Ripper. Once again, we have a book where chapter after chapter is action packed. There is NO FILLER in thi</span>
  <span id="freeText6537727755348617244" style="display:none">LIVE ON AMAZON! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00CRJNH9I?ie=UTF8&amp;force-full-site=1&amp;ref_=aw_bottom_links">http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00C...</a><br /><br />When I first read UnDeniable I thought, now here is a book that is honest, raw and a true page-turner. I honestly didn’t think Madeline could top herself. I mean, if you’ve read UnDeniable, you know what I mean. <b>
  <u>I.WAS.WRONG.</u>
</b><br /><br />UnBeautifully is the heart wrenching, scarred, frustrating, intense and ultimately <b>BEAUTIFUL</b> story of Danny &amp; Ripper. Once again, we have a book where chapter after chapter is action packed. There is NO FILLER in this book. Every single word written is relevant and important. I really wanted to take my time and soak in all that is happening – and trust me, there is SO much going on. <br /><br />In UnBeautifully, you get the POV’s of Danny, Ripper, Eva &amp; Deuce. In my mind, that was a GENIUS move. You get to be inside the head of all 4 of them and this gives you such a great perspective. There were times while reading that I just felt SO DEEPLY their emotions &amp; got so connected to each and every character. Madeline is truly a talented writer to be able to suck me in and feel so much for these fictional characters that she has brought to life for me. <br /><br />I’m truly honored that Madeline allowed me to read/review this early. She pours her heart, soul, blood and tears into EVERY book she writes and it shows – BOY OH BOY does it show. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>THANK YOU MADELINE SHEEHAN FOR SHARING THIS FUCKING AWESOME MASTERPIECE.</u>
</b> <br /><br />*More reviews available at <a href="http://www.lovenbooks.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Love N. Books</a></span>

<div id="review_619247223" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/619247223" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/619247223?book_show_action=true">May 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer619247223" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3997022607868323384">4 HELL'S HORSEMAN STARS.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422141i/839540._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Where do I begin to talk about my feelings for this story. I'm not sure there are words to fit, I'm exhausted after my Madeline Sheehan book workout. This author certainly knows how to draw out every single emotion possible from her readers. I think I'll start where the other did with the most enchanting prologue I've ever read ...<br/><br/><i>
  <b>“Love is a feeling, a real, raw, and unscripted emotion so sensationally pure, unable to dull even under the strain of a world against it, s</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText3997022607868323384" style="display:none">4 HELL'S HORSEMAN STARS.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422141i/839540._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Where do I begin to talk about my feelings for this story. I'm not sure there are words to fit, I'm exhausted after my Madeline Sheehan book workout. This author certainly knows how to draw out every single emotion possible from her readers. I think I'll start where the other did with the most enchanting prologue I've ever read ...<br><br><i>
  <b>“Love is a feeling, a real, raw, and unscripted emotion so sensationally pure, unable to dull even under the strain of a world against it, strong enough to heal the broken and warm even the coldest of hearts. <br>Innate.<br>Unavoidable.<br>Undeniable.<br>And sometimes, love is unconventional and it breaks all the rules and blurs all the lines and basks in its glory, shining as bright as the sun, unapologetically glowing even under the narrowed stares of society and its screaming, self-righteous morals, berating and judging that which it doesn’t understand.”</b>
</i><br><br>'Unbeautifully' is unbelievably raw, moving, emotional, gritty, gut wrenching, soul searching, intense, perfectly flawed and filled to the brim and over flowing with Horseman style drama.<br><br>This is a powerful, ugly, yet somehow beautiful tale of life, love and loyalty. Once again the author takes the reader front and centre stage into the lives of the Hell's Horseman Motorcycle club.<br><br>Danielle 'Danny' west daughter of the president of the notorious club is having difficulties finding her own way in life, everything seems to falling apart around her, throw into the mix her attraction for Erik 'Ripper' Jacobs, Sergeant in arms for the club and you've got the start of a tale of two with plenty to keep you entertained in between.<br><br>Ripper is carrying the burden of a past that has left him disfigured angry and unable to move forward. This unbeautifully, beautiful couple find a way to erase what should not be,and find comfort and hope with each other, but completing this journey takes more than its toll. An epic story of love and the aching possibility of a future for Danny and Ripper - pain, heartache and trials follow this couple like a curse and my heart was hanging on to all hope that it would be worth it for this couple to be together right till the last page.<br><br>This story is an eye opener and packs a lot into four plus hours of reading. The story is certainly not for the faint hearted. The author sums up the warning of what the book entails so I suggest you check that out before reading. <br><br>My final thoughts:<br>This novel hosts a book full of regrets, pain and ugly truths, it highlights a world of brutality and a community of men and women who fight hard for their survival and people they love.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380422141i/839541._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All in all Strangely I was enthralled with this gritty love tale and i devoured it in one sitting, I'm looking forward to see what this author will do next. There is no doubt that this author can write, as a taster check out these 'unbeautifully' beautiful quotes:<br><br>❤❤“Baby,” he said, “listen to me. I ain’t beautiful, you are. You’re so damn beautiful you got it spillin’ out all over the place, blindin’ you into thinkin’ I’m beautiful when I ain’t. Farthest thing from it.” <br><br>❤❤“Ripper was my rainstorm, my skin-drenching frenzy, where you couldn’t tell right from left, where all you could feel was the phenomenon exploding throughout your body, feverishly burning through you even as it pleasurably cooled.” <br><br>❤❤“All scars tell a story beautiful girl....mine tell the story of how I found you.” <br><br>❤❤“You’re my reason, Deuce … You always have been.” <br><br>4 RIPPER AND DANNY STARS.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3997022607868323384" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_453486985" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/453486985" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10149843-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593628440p2/10149843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/453486985?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/10149843-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10149843-sarah?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10149843-sarah?shelf=unforgettable">unforgettable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453486985" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17686319860086722736"><br/><b>*Full Spoiler free review - apart from quotes* <br/><br/><br/>Five......'Holy fuckin' cow, what did I just read?, can I have my mind back please?........well deserved stars....</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&current=cd5c91fc43fb947cb23540e905e28088_zps8f5dbab1.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397268i/766384._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Are there any words to describe the feelings I had reading this book? How can an author have the ability to write about things in life that on the surface can only be described as raw and ugly nightmares, but yet she somehow turns them into something 'beautiful'?<br/><br/>'Unbeautifully' is Ripper and Danny's story. It's not a fairy tale story</span>
  <span id="freeText17686319860086722736" style="display:none"><br><b>*Full Spoiler free review - apart from quotes* <br><br><br>Five......'Holy fuckin' cow, what did I just read?, can I have my mind back please?........well deserved stars....</b><br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=cd5c91fc43fb947cb23540e905e28088_zps8f5dbab1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397268i/766384._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Are there any words to describe the feelings I had reading this book? How can an author have the ability to write about things in life that on the surface can only be described as raw and ugly nightmares, but yet she somehow turns them into something 'beautiful'?<br><br>'Unbeautifully' is Ripper and Danny's story. It's not a fairy tale story. its not a 'boy meets girl, boy falls in love with girl, and they ride off into the sunset. It's not about hearts and flowers or sweet love songs. As the author warned very clearly at the beginning.....<b>"this is a story about pain, sorrow, and suffering......love blossoms in a secret world full of crime, violence, and death" </b><br><br>Like 'Undeniable', it's a story full of bad mouthed, dirty talking bikers, and therefore, as expected, these bikers live in a world where drama follows them around. Bikers who certainly take the term 'alpha male' to a totally different level. Ripper and Danny's story is as the author warns <b>"about what can be born from nightmares"</b>... And I have to say I loved every freaking minute of this crazy arsed ride!!!<br><br>Ripper and Danny's story started where 'Undeniable' left us. It's the story of Danny; young, beautiful, sweet daughter of Deuce, the president of the Hell's Horsemen Motor Cycle club. Danny, who despite growing up surrounded by tough biker men is still living a fairly innocent, carefree life, a life that includes high school proms and 'hello Kitty' merchandise.<br><br>It's also the story of Ripper, broken and now scarred, both on the inside and on the outside, Sergeant of Arms in the Hell’s Horsemen MC Club, who's life has become that of nightmares, a life full of trauma. <br><br>You couldn't have two more different people, one is like the sunshine and one is like the shadows but what happens when the sunshine and the shadows collide? <br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=93a67ac0adec285ae9644c71aa8d3eae_zpsda655fa1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397268i/766385._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What happens when Ripper, the man who was ready and willing to die, who has tasted nothing but pain for what seems like an eternity suddenly gets a taste of something sweet?<br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=a05621f34970dbfbaa6c65b07e0c52a3_zpsa0abfb67.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397268i/766386._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Please believe me when I say if you are looking for lovey, dovey romance, roses and white picket fences and love scenes that are sweet and tender...... then you're looking in the wrong place. This is a beautifully written love story, a love story that will pull you in and hold onto to you until the very end. But its not a love story in any conventional sense. It's laced with pain, suffering and loss. There is a whole lot of drama and lots of intense, animalistic fucking but lets be realistic here....this is a motor cycle club and these are bad mouthed bikers who are part of the criminal underworld....... so it was never going to be the next Romeo and Juliet!!!!. <br><br>Things happened in this story that shocked me, things happened that broke my heart, things happened that I could not remotely understand nor connect with and some things happened that I unfortunately could. This author has written a story that will challenge many people's views, a story that is both thought provoking and so utterly gripping but wether you as a reader agree with the things that occur or not, underneath it all, it was a love story. <br><br>A love story that reminded me that life isn't aways a fairy tale, nothing is ever straightforward, people are forced to make difficult and hurtful decisions, and people make both right and wrong choices but sometimes <b> if you want to see the rainbow, you have to get though a shit load of rain.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=346831f0598624984d0fd99e98439f45_zps3dce4da7.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397268i/766387._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Just sit back and enjoy the ride baby!!!!!! <br><br><a href="http://s1352.photobucket.com/albums/q659/Zippy1980/?action=view&amp;current=ec5d1482b37e63914bff20449f249c91_zpsa2cdbd7c.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397268i/766388._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Thanks to my Haven Hotties for reading Danny and Rippers story with me x♥x<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17686319860086722736" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
