<div id="review_1801451740" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1801451740" />
    <a title="NMmomof4" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4"><img alt="NMmomof4" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515474309p2/24665574.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1801451740?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NMmomof4" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NMmomof4" href="/user/show/24665574-nmmomof4">NMmomof4</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=disordered-mc">disordered-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=separation-with-other-partners">separation-with-other-partners</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=mc">mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=not-safe">not-safe</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=unlikely-couple">unlikely-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=tears">tears</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24665574-nmmomof4?shelf=taboo">taboo</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1801451740" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2212011159768901783"><b> 4 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was an enjoyable read. If you want a grittier mc romance, this series is what you need! It definitely isn't rainbows and unicorns, but I still enjoyed it. There were some actions by the h that ticked me off, but otherwise I thought that the angst and connections were pretty spot on. This has a good bit of connection to the first book, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16109563.Undeniable__Undeniable___1_' title='Undeniable (Undeniable, #1) by Madeline Sheehan' rel='nofollow noopener'>Undeniable</a>, because we get a lot of what is going on with Deuce and Eva in this one. I'm pretty sure this can be read as a stand alo</span>
  <span id="freeText2212011159768901783" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> This was an enjoyable read. If you want a grittier mc romance, this series is what you need! It definitely isn't rainbows and unicorns, but I still enjoyed it. There were some actions by the h that ticked me off, but otherwise I thought that the angst and connections were pretty spot on. This has a good bit of connection to the first book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16109563.Undeniable__Undeniable___1_" title="Undeniable (Undeniable, #1) by Madeline Sheehan" rel="nofollow noopener">Undeniable</a>, because we get a lot of what is going on with Deuce and Eva in this one. I'm pretty sure this can be read as a stand alone, but I would recommend reading the first book to fully understand the dynamics in this one (and it was good anyways IMO and only $0.99 on Amazon right now ;D).<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Danny and Ripper's story. Danny is the mc president's daughter, and Ripper is sent to pick her up from her disastrous prom. One thing led to another, and they end up spending the night together. Neither of them can deny the pull that they feel from that night, and they eventually give in and have a secret affair. There is some family and club drama, some hot sexy times, and a few sad and sweet moments too...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between focusing on Danny, Ripper, Deuce, and Eva in 3rd person narrative. I did find it kind of odd that there was as much focus on Deuce and Eva as there was, but it worked somehow...<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I did skim very briefly during the club drama, but that is definitely a "just me" thing (because I always seem to do that with mc romances)! I thought it flowed well overall.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Kind of. They connect instantly once they become physical, but I felt like it a was believable progression into stronger feelings.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 3.5 stars. Ripper. I felt really bad for his past trauma, and I liked the way he loved the h. I do wish he <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[kept it in his pants during their separation  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3 stars. Danny. I liked her, but then I had BIG issues with how she handled the H's return and treated ZZ. <br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low/moderate. I teared up a few times, but I never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H is adamantly against coming out with their relationship, so in a way he pushes the h away emotionally. The H also pushes her away when some big drama goes down. They both pursue the relationship at times. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate. They have some hot chemistry and scenes, but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes and no. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Mentions of birth control and condom use (not always). The H mentioned never being without a condom, but no mention that I remember about the h's past practices (she does use a condom with OM) or STD statuses. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h does end up unexpectedly pregnant and has an abortion during their separation  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h is another man's old lady when the H returns, and this causes a lot of drama. The H had a club whore that he was regularly with in the past, and she causes some drama too. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There is a descriptive scene of the h and OM. There is mentions of the H's sexual activities, but I don't remember any descriptive details. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The h is another man's old lady when the H returns and she sleeps with the H. So, she cheated on the OM in my book. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ They are separated for ~1 year. They both have other partners during this time (H hooks up randomly and h becomes another man's old lady).  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ 14 year age difference between h and H, H had been mutilated with a knife and is missing an eye (flashbacks), rape (flashbacks), violence/murder/drugs (harder but typical mc stuff), unexpected pregnancy, and abortion. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b>This had a cute jump ahead epilogue with a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I paid the $3.99 on Amazon.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one is probably <u>Not Safe</u> for the safety gals.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does </b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does </b> have a descriptive sex scene with h and OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the H pushing the h away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a ~1 year separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does </b> have abuse (not by mcs)<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="2212011159768901783" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer451234882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12551061372468361266"><br/><b>“He wasn’t the kind of guy you went to dinner and a movie with. He was the kind of guy who dragged you out of the lake, shoved you down on the ground, growling and groping you, telling you all the dirty things he wanted to do to you…and then did them."</b><br/><br/><blockquote>HELL YEAH...that's what I'm talking about!!!!!!!!!!</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396930ra/765493.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ripper........he is scarred up physically and emotionally. He is a badass biker and he is soooooooo damn fine!!!!!!!!! I can't even elaborate much more but I will tell you this scars or no scars th</span>
  <span id="freeText12551061372468361266" style="display:none"><br><b>“He wasn’t the kind of guy you went to dinner and a movie with. He was the kind of guy who dragged you out of the lake, shoved you down on the ground, growling and groping you, telling you all the dirty things he wanted to do to you…and then did them."</b><br><br><blockquote>HELL YEAH...that's what I'm talking about!!!!!!!!!!</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396930ra/765493.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ripper........he is scarred up physically and emotionally. He is a badass biker and he is soooooooo damn fine!!!!!!!!! I can't even elaborate much more but I will tell you this scars or no scars that man is HAWT!!!!!!!<br> <br>Danny........The MC President's daughter. She young, cute and in love with a bad boy!!!!!!!<br><br><b>“Ours was the furthest thing from a picture-perfect romance; it was more of a car crash, a metal-bending, blood-splattered disaster that left no survivors, only bad memories and heartache. But it was ours."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396930i/765494.jpg" width="600" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Is this book a hearts and flower romance novel.........<b>Hell No It's Not!!!</b><br><br>Is this book as psycho crazy and Deuce and Eva's book.......<b>Sadly no!!!!!</b><br><br>So what is this book? This book is a great love story about looking past what is on the outside and loving a person for what they are not what they look like. <br><br><b>"Everything has beauty. Even the ugly. Especially the ugly.<br>Because without ugly there would be no beauty.<br>Because without beauty we would not survive our pain, our sorrow, and our suffering. And in the world I lived in, the world he lived in, a secret world within the world, a world of of constant crime and cruel, cold, death, there was almost nothing but suffering."</b><br><br>This book is the 2nd book in this series I absolutely love all these characters. I was so happy and sad to get to see Deuce and Eva again......they have been through some rough times. I was kind of hoping for another crazy book like Undeniable but I will say this book fit these two characters perfectly. I can't wait for the next book!!!<br><br>If you haven't started this series yet GET ON IT!!!!!!!!!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396930i/765495.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Scars or not I love you Ripper....and I don't care how many spoilers V has to hide stuff in, I will out right say it...you are <b>MINE:))))</b><br><br><b>Buddy read with Vishous and Rachel!!!!!!</b></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('G+O9JkaXynOIYp0QHpvisxQG54ak7po1704U2Wk5nK0Eu4jXElVnwIh/WLgfrnLCG2+BTsTlBppkyMUZRj457w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('fzKExZhqDSgNOghpwDYPeDHIJbkEviP8saRIP8uGob9garE0zKigmw0nzcHBA58JPqFDcWS1v1M6Ipn/5IEE/Q==')})
  }

Days later, his family and friends should have been picking up the pieces, moving on. Instead, they’ve been catapulted into a world so twisted and dangerous even the most ruthless among them would be stunned to discover the tangled web of deception, not only on the dangerous streets of South Florida but all the way to the top.  In this gripping follow-up novel to Nine Minutes, Out of Time takes readers from the sun-drenched flatlands of 1950s Central Florida to the vivid tropical heat of Fort Lauderdale to the halls of Florida’s Death Row as we finally learn the gritty backstory of Jason “Grizz” Talbot and the secret he spent his life trying to conceal.  Not even Grizz’s inner circle knows his full story—the tragedy that enveloped his early life, the surprise discovery that made him the government’s most wanted and most feared, and the depths of his love for Ginny, the tenderhearted innocent he’d once abducted and later made his wife.  Once Grizz’s obsession and now the mother of his child, Ginny has spent years grieving the man she’d first resisted and then came to love. Now remarried to Tommy, a former member of the gang, the pair have spent more than a decade trying desperately to live a normal existence far from the violent, crime-ridden world they’d once carved out on the edge of the Florida Everglades. For Tommy, especially, the stakes are high. Desperately in love with Ginny for years, he’s finally living his dream: married to the woman he never thought he could have. But even with the façade of normalcy—thriving careers, two beautiful children, and a genuinely happy and loving marriage—they can’t seem to put the past behind them. Every time they turn around, another secret is revealed, unraveling the very bonds that hold them together.  And with Grizz finally put to death, now Ginny has learned secrets so dark, so evil she’s not even sure she can go on.  Will these secrets tear their love to pieces?             <span class="readable">&ldquo;Love is a feeling, a real, raw, and unscripted emotion so sensationally pure, unable to dull even under the strain of a world against it, strong enough to heal the broken and warm even the coldest of hearts. <br />Innate.<br />Unavoidable.<br /><i>Undeniable.</i><br />And sometimes, love is unconventional and it breaks all the rules and blurs all the lines and basks in its glory, shining as bright as the sun, unapologetically glowing even under the narrowed stares of society and its screaming, self-righteous morals, berating and judging that which it doesn’t understand.&rdquo;</span>
